## 🔧 Comandos Disponíveis

```bash
# Desenvolvimento
npm run dev              # Inicia servidor de desenvolvimento
npm run dev:debug        # Inicia com debug habilitado

# Banco de Dados
npm run db:migrate       # Executa migrações
npm run db:rollback      # Reverte última migração
npm run db:seed          # Popula banco com dados de teste
npm run db:reset         # Reseta banco completamente

# Testes
npm test                 # Executa todos os testes
npm run test:unit        # Apenas testes unitários
npm run test:integration # Apenas testes de integração
npm run test:e2e         # Apenas testes end-to-end
npm run test:coverage    # Testes com cobertura

# Qualidade de Código
npm run lint             # Executa linter
npm run lint:fix         # Corrige problemas de linting
npm run format           # Formata código com Prettier

# Build e Deploy
npm run build            # Compila para produção
npm run start            # Inicia em produção
npm run docker:build     # Build da imagem Docker
npm run docker:run       # Executa container Docker

# Modo Hive
npm run hive:start       # Inicia modo Hive
npm run hive:status      # Status dos agentes
npm run hive:stop        # Para modo Hive
```

## 📚 Documentação da API

A API segue o padrão RESTful e está documentada com OpenAPI 3.0.

### Acessando a Documentação

1. **Swagger UI**: `http://localhost:3000/api-docs`
2. **OpenAPI JSON**: `http://localhost:3000/api-docs/json`
3. **Postman Collection**: Disponível em `docs/api/postman-collection.json`

### Autenticação

```http
POST /api/v1/auth/login
Content-Type: application/json

{
  "email": "admin@diyapp.com",
  "password": "securepassword"
}

Response:
{
  "success": true,
  "data": {
    "token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9...",
    "user": {
      "id": 1,
      "email": "admin@diyapp.com",
      "role": "admin"
    }
  }
}
```

Use o token JWT no header das requisições:
```http
Authorization: Bearer <seu_token_jwt>
```

### Endpoints Principais

#### Tarefas (Tasks)

```http
GET /api/v1/tasks
```
Lista todas as tarefas com paginação.

**Query Parameters:**
- `page` (number): Página atual (padrão: 1)
- `limit` (number): Itens por página (padrão: 20)
- `status` (string): Filtrar por status
- `agentId` (number): Filtrar por agente

```http
POST /api/v1/tasks
Content-Type: application/json

{
  "title": "Implementar feature X",
  "description": "Descrição detalhada da tarefa",
  "priority": "high",
  "estimatedHours": 8,
  "assignedAgentId": 3,
  "projectId": 1
}
```

```http
GET /api/v1/tasks/:id
```
Obtém detalhes de uma tarefa específica.

```http
PUT /api/v1/tasks/:id
Content-Type: application/json

{
  "status": "in_progress",
  "progress": 50
}
```

```http
DELETE /api/v1/tasks/:id
```
Remove uma tarefa (soft delete).

#### Agentes (Agents)

```http
GET /api/v1/agents
```
Lista todos os agentes disponíveis.

```http
POST /api/v1/agents
Content-Type: application/json

{
  "name": "Tech Writer",
  "type": "tech_writer",
  "specialization": "documentation",
  "maxConcurrentTasks": 3,
  "config": {
    "documentationStandards": "markdown",
    "autoAudit": true
  }
}
```

```http
PUT /api/v1/agents/:id/activate
```
Ativa um agente para receber tarefas.

```http
PUT /api/v1/agents/:id/deactivate
```
Desativa um agente temporariamente.

#### Modo Hive

```http
POST /api/v1/hive/tasks
Content-Type: application/json

{
  "projectId": 1,
  "tasks": [
    {
      "type": "refactor",
      "target": "src/api/controllers/userController.js",
      "priority": "medium"
    },
    {
      "type": "documentation",
      "target": "README.md",
      "priority": "high"
    }
  ],
  "parallelism": 3,
  "timeout": 300000
}
```

**Response:**
```json
{
  "success": true,
  "data": {
    "hiveSessionId": "hive_123456",
    "totalTasks": 2,
    "assignedAgents": 2,
    "estimatedCompletion": "2024-01-15T14:30:00Z"
  }
}
```

```http
GET /api/v1/hive/sessions/:sessionId
```
Monitora o progresso de uma sessão Hive.

```http
GET /api/v1/hive/sessions/:sessionId/conflicts
```
Lista conflitos detectados durante execução paralela.

### Códigos de Status

- `200 OK`: Requisição bem-sucedida
- `201 Created`: Recurso criado com sucesso
- `400 Bad Request`: Dados inválidos
- `401 Unauthorized`: Autenticação necessária
- `403 Forbidden`: Permissão insuficiente
- `404 Not Found`: Recurso não encontrado
- `409 Conflict`: Conflito de dados
- `422 Unprocessable Entity`: Validação falhou
- `429 Too Many Requests`: Rate limit excedido
- `500 Internal Server Error`: Erro no servidor
- `503 Service Unavailable`: Serviço indisponível

### Rate Limiting

- 100 requisições por minuto por IP
- 1000 requisições por hora por usuário autenticado
- Headers de resposta:
  - `X-RateLimit-Limit`: Limite total
  - `X-RateLimit-Remaining`: Requisições restantes
  - `X-RateLimit-Reset`: Timestamp de reset

## 🤖 Modo Hive - Execução Paralela

O Modo Hive permite que múltiplos agentes trabalhem em paralelo no mesmo projeto, com mecanismos de resolução de conflitos automáticos.

### Como Funciona

1. **Orquestração**: O Hive Orchestrator divide o trabalho em tarefas independentes
2. **Distribuição**: Tarefas são atribuídas a agentes especializados
3. **Execução Paralela**: Agentes trabalham simultaneamente
4. **Detecção de Conflitos**: Sistema identifica conflitos em tempo real
5. **Resolução Automática**: Conflitos são resolvidos seguindo regras predefinidas
6. **Merge Controlado**: Mudanças são integradas de forma segura

### Configuração do Hive

```javascript
// src/hive/config.js
module.exports = {
  maxParallelAgents: 5,
  taskTimeout: 300000, // 5 minutos
  conflictResolution: {
    strategy: 'auto_merge', // auto_merge, manual, vote
    autoMergeRules: {
      documentation: 'always', // Documentação sempre mescla
      testFiles: 'if_passes', // Testes só se passarem
      coreLogic: 'manual'     // Lógica core requer revisão
    },
    fallbackTo: 'tech_lead'   // Fallback para Tech Lead
  },
  rollbackOnFailure: true,
  auditTrail: true
};
```

### Monitoramento

Acesse o dashboard Hive em: `http://localhost:3000/hive-dashboard`

## 🧪 Testes

### Estrutura de Testes

```bash
tests/
├── unit/           # Testes unitários
│   ├── agents/     # Testes de agentes
│   ├── services/   # Testes de serviços
│   └── utils/      # Testes de utilitários
├── integration/    # Testes de integração
│   ├── api/        # Testes de API
│   └── hive/       # Testes do Modo Hive
└── e2e/            # Testes end-to-end
    ├── workflows/  # Fluxos de trabalho
    └── ui/         # Testes de interface
```

### Executando Testes

```bash
# Todos os testes
npm test

# Testes com cobertura
npm run test:coverage

# Testes específicos
npm test -- --grep "Modo Hive"

# Watch mode (desenvolvimento)
npm run test:watch
```

### Exemplo de Teste

```javascript
// tests/unit/services/task-service.test.js
const TaskService = require('../../../src/services/task-service');
const { Task } = require('../../../src/models');

describe('TaskService', () => {
  describe('createTask', () => {
    it('deve criar uma tarefa com dados válidos', async () => {
      const taskData = {
        title: 'Nova tarefa',
        description: 'Descrição da tarefa',
        priority: 'medium'
      };
      
      const task = await TaskService.createTask(taskData);
      
      expect(task).toHaveProperty('id');
      expect(task.title).toBe(taskData.title);
      expect(task.status).toBe('pending');
    });
    
    it('deve lançar erro para dados inválidos', async () => {
      await expect(TaskService.createTask({}))
        .rejects
        .toThrow('Title is required');
    });
  });
});
```

## 🐳 Docker

### Build e Execução

```bash
# Build da imagem
docker build -t diyapp-v11 .

# Executar container
docker run -d \
  --name diyapp-v11 \
  -p 3000:3000 \
  -v $(pwd)/data:/app/data \
  -v $(pwd)/logs:/app/logs \
  --env-file .env \
  diyapp-v11

# Docker Compose (recomendado)
docker-compose up -d
```

### docker-compose.yml

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  app:
    build: .
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - DB_TYPE=postgres
      - DB_HOST=postgres
      - DB_PORT=5432
      - DB_NAME=diyapp_v11
      - DB_USER=postgres
      - DB_PASSWORD=${DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - ./data:/app/data
      - ./logs:/app/logs
    depends_on:
      - postgres
    restart: unless-stopped

  postgres:
    image: postgres:14-alpine
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_DB=diyapp_v11
      - POSTGRES_USER=postgres
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    restart: unless-stopped

volumes:
  postgres_data:
```

## 📊 Monitoramento e Logs

### Logs Estruturados

```javascript
// Exemplo de log
{
  "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",
  "level": "info",
  "message": "Task completed successfully",
  "agentId": "tech_writer_001",
  "taskId": "task_123456",
  "duration": 45000,
  "hiveSessionId": "hive_789012",
  "metadata": {
    "documentationType": "api",
    "linesAdded": 150,
    "conflictsResolved": 2
  }
}
```

### Métricas Coletadas

- Tempo de resposta da API
- Uso de CPU/memória dos agentes
- Taxa de conclusão de tarefas
- Conflitos detectados/resolvidos
- Erros por agente/tipo

GET /health
```
**Response:**
```json
{
  "status": "healthy",
  "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",
  "services": {
    "database": "connected",
    "hive": "active

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core: Otimização de Performance

Vou configurar um sistema completo de otimização de performance com análise estática, otimização de bundles, caching estratégico e monitoramento de métricas.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-performance/
├── package.json
├── .eslintrc.js
├── .sonar-project.properties
├── sonar-scanner.js
├── webpack.config.js

```javascript
module.exports = {
  env: {
    browser: true,
    es2021: true,
    node: true,
    jest: true
  },
  extends: [
    'eslint:recommended',
    'plugin:react/recommended',
    'plugin:@typescript-eslint/recommended',
    'airbnb',
    'plugin:sonarjs/recommended'
  ],
  parser: '@typescript-eslint/parser',
  parserOptions: {
    ecmaFeatures: {
      jsx: true
    },
    ecmaVersion: 'latest',
    sourceType: 'module'
  },
  plugins: [
    'react',
    '@typescript-eslint',
    'react-hooks',
    'sonarjs'
  ],
  rules: {
    // Performance-related rules
    'react/jsx-no-bind': ['error', {
      allowArrowFunctions: true,
      allowBind: false,
      ignoreRefs: true
    }],
    'react/no-unused-prop-types': 'error',
    'react/require-default-props': 'off',
    'react/jsx-props-no-spreading': 'off',
    'import/no-extraneous-dependencies': ['error', {
      devDependencies: true
    }],
    'no-console': ['warn', {
      allow: ['warn', 'error', 'info']
    }],
    'no-debugger': 'warn',
    'max-len': ['error', {
      code: 100,
      ignoreComments: true,
      ignoreUrls: true,
      ignoreTemplateLiterals: true
    }],
    'complexity': ['error', 10],
    'max-depth': ['error', 4],
    'max-params': ['error', 4],
    'sonarjs/cognitive-complexity': ['error', 15],
    'sonarjs/no-duplicate-string': 'error',
    'sonarjs/no-identical-functions': 'error',

      argsIgnorePattern: '^_'

    react: {
      version: 'detect'

## 3. .sonar-project.properties

```properties
# SonarQube Configuration for DIYAPP V11
sonar.projectKey=diyapp-v11-performance
sonar.projectName=DIYAPP Evolution V11 - Performance Core
sonar.projectVersion=1.0.0
sonar.sources=src
sonar.tests=tests
sonar.sourceEncoding=UTF-8
sonar.exclusions=**/node_modules/**, **/dist/**, **/coverage/**, **/*.test.js, **/*.spec.js
sonar.test.inclusions=**/*.test.js, **/*.spec.js
sonar.javascript.lcov.reportPaths=coverage/lcov.info
sonar.qualitygate.wait=true

# Performance Metrics Thresholds
sonar.javascript.complexity.threshold=10
sonar.javascript.functionComplexity.threshold=5
sonar.javascript.fileComplexity.threshold=15
sonar.javascript.duplicatedLines.threshold=3
sonar.javascript.cognitiveComplexity.threshold=15

# Security Rules
sonar.security.repositories=php-security-checker,findsecbugs
sonar.security.configuration=security-config.json

# Coverage
sonar.coverage.exclusions=**/*.d.ts,**/index.js,**/serviceWorker.js
```

## 4. sonar-scanner.js

```javascript
#!/usr/bin/env node

const scanner = require('sonarqube-scanner');
const path = require('path');
const fs = require('fs');

// Read package.json for version info
const packageJson = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(path.join(__dirname, 'package.json'), 'utf8'));

scanner(
  {
    serverUrl: process.env.SONARQUBE_URL || 'http://localhost:9000',
    token: process.env.SONARQUBE_TOKEN || '',
    options: {
      'sonar.projectKey': 'diyapp-v11-performance',
      'sonar.projectName': packageJson.name,
      'sonar.projectVersion': packageJson.version,
      'sonar.projectDescription': packageJson.description,
      'sonar.sources': 'src',
      'sonar.tests': 'tests',
      'sonar.sourceEncoding': 'UTF-8',
      'sonar.exclusions': '**/node_modules/**, **/dist/**, **/coverage/**, **/*.test.js, **/*.spec.js',
      'sonar.test.inclusions': '**/*.test.js, **/*.spec.js',
      'sonar.javascript.lcov.reportPaths': 'coverage/lcov.info',
      'sonar.javascript.file.suffixes': '.js,.jsx,.ts,.tsx',
      'sonar.typescript.tsconfigPath': 'tsconfig.json',
      'sonar.qualitygate.wait': true,
      'sonar.qualitygate.timeout': 300,
      
      // Performance thresholds
      'sonar.javascript.complexity.threshold': '10',
      'sonar.javascript.functionComplexity.threshold': '5',
      'sonar.javascript.fileComplexity.threshold': '15',
      'sonar.javascript.cognitiveComplexity.threshold': '15',
      'sonar.javascript.duplicatedLines.threshold': '3',
      
      // Security
      'sonar.security.configuration': 'security-config.json',
    },
  },
  () => process.exit()
);
```

## 5. vite.config.js

```javascript
import { defineConfig } from 'vite';
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react';
import { VitePWA } from 'vite-plugin-pwa';
import compression from 'vite-plugin-compression';
import { visualizer } from 'rollup-plugin-visualizer';
import path from 'path';

// https://vitejs.dev/config/
export default defineConfig(({ mode }) => ({
  base: '/',
  plugins: [
    react({
      jsxImportSource: '@emotion/react',
      babel: {
        plugins: ['@emotion/babel-plugin'],
      },
    }),
    VitePWA({
      registerType: 'autoUpdate',
      includeAssets: ['favicon.ico', 'robots.txt', 'apple-touch-icon.png'],
      manifest: {
        name: 'DIYAPP V11 Performance',
        short_name: 'DIYAPP V11',
        description: 'High-performance application with P95 < 200ms',
        theme_color: '#ffffff',
        icons: [
          {
            src: 'pwa-192x192.png',
            sizes: '192x192',
            type: 'image/png',
          },
          {
            src: 'pwa-512x512.png',
            sizes: '512x512',
            type: 'image/png',
          },
        ],
      },
      workbox: {
        globPatterns: ['**/*.{js,css,html,ico,png,svg,woff2}'],
        runtimeCaching: [
          {
            urlPattern: /^https:\/\/api\./,
            handler: 'NetworkFirst',
            options: {
              cacheName: 'api-cache',
              expiration: {
                maxEntries: 100,
                maxAgeSeconds: 60 * 60 * 24, // 24 hours
              },
            },
          },
          {
            urlPattern: /\.(?:png|jpg|jpeg|svg|gif)$/,
            handler: 'CacheFirst',
            options: {
              cacheName: 'image-cache',
              expiration: {
                maxEntries: 100,
                maxAgeSeconds: 60 * 60 * 24 * 7, // 7 days
              },
            },
          },
        ],
      },
    }),
    compression({
      algorithm: 'gzip',
      ext: '.gz',
      threshold: 10240,
    }),
    compression({
      algorithm: 'brotliCompress',
      ext: '.br',
    }),
    mode === 'analyze' && visualizer({
      filename: './dist/bundle-analysis.html',
      open: true,
      gzipSize: true,
      brotliSize: true,
    }),
  ].filter(Boolean),
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@': path.resolve(__dirname, './src'),
      '@components': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/components'),
      '@utils': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/utils'),
      '@api': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/api'),
    },
  },
  build: {
    outDir: 'dist',
    sourcemap: mode !== 'production',
    minify: 'terser',
    terserOptions: {
      compress: {
        drop_console: mode === 'production',
        drop_debugger: mode === 'production',
      },
    },
    rollupOptions: {
      output: {
        manualChunks: {
          vendor: ['react', 'react-dom', 'react-router-dom'],
          utils: ['axios', 'lodash-es'],
          ui: ['@emotion/react', '@emotion/styled'],
        },
        chunkFileNames: 'assets/js/[name]-[hash].js',
        entryFileNames: 'assets/js/[name]-[hash].js',
        assetFileNames: 'assets/[ext]/[name]-[hash].[ext]',
      },
    },
    chunkSizeWarningLimit: 1000,
  },
  server: {
    port: 3000,
    host: true,
    open: true,
    cors: true,
    headers: {
      'Cache-Control': 'public, max-age=31536000',
    },
  },
  preview: {
    port: 3001,
    host: true,
  },
  optimizeDeps: {
    include: ['react', 'react-dom', 'react-router-dom'],
    exclude: ['@emotion/react'],
  },
}));
```

## 6. src/index.html

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <meta name="description" content="DIYAPP Evolution V11 - High Performance Application">
    <title>DIYAPP V11 - Performance Dashboard</title>
    
    <!-- Preload critical resources -->
    <link rel="preload" href="/src/styles/main.css" as="style">
    <link rel="preload" href="/src/main.js" as="script">
    
    <!-- Preconnect to APIs -->
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://api.diyapp.com">
    <link rel="dns-prefetch" href="https://api.diyapp.com">
    
    <!-- Performance monitoring -->
    <script>
        // Performance monitoring script
        (function() {
            window.performanceMetrics = {
                startTime: performance.now(),
                marks: {},
                measures: {},
                
                mark: function(name) {
                    this.marks[name] = performance.now();
                    performance.mark(name);
                },
                
                measure: function(name, startMark, endMark) {
                    this.measures[name] = performance.measure(name, startMark, endMark);
                },
                
                getMetrics: function() {
                    const navigation = performance.getEntriesByType('navigation')[0];
                    const paint = performance.getEntriesByType('paint');
                    const resources = performance.getEntriesByType('resource');
                    
                    return {
                        navigation: navigation ? {
                            domComplete: navigation.domComplete,
                            domInteractive: navigation.domInteractive,
                            loadEventEnd: navigation.loadEventEnd,
                            domContentLoadedEventEnd: navigation.domContentLoadedEventEnd,
                            firstPaint: paint.find(p => p.name === 'first-paint')?.startTime,
                            firstContentfulPaint: paint.find(p => p.name === 'first-contentful-paint')?.startTime,
                            largestContentfulPaint: performance.getEntriesByType('largest-contentful-paint')[0]?.startTime,
                            cumulativeLayoutShift: performance.getEntriesByType('layout-shift').reduce((sum, entry) => sum + entry.value, 0)
                        } : null,
                        resources: resources.map(r => ({
                            name: r.name,
                            duration: r.duration,
                            transferSize: r.transferSize,
                            initiatorType: r.initiatorType
                        })),
                        marks: this.marks,
                        measures: this.measures
                    };
                }
            };
            
            // Mark initial load
            window.performanceMetrics.mark('pageStart');
            
            // Report Web Vitals
            if ('webVitals' in window) {
                webVitals.getCLS(console.log);
                webVitals.getFID(console.log);
                webVitals.getFCP(console.log);
                webVitals

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Modelagem de Dados

## 1. Schema do Banco de Dados (PostgreSQL)

### 1.1. Tabelas Principais

```sql
-- ============================================
-- SCHEMA: diyapp_v11
-- VERSÃO: 1.0.0
-- DESCRIÇÃO: Schema principal do DIYAPP Evolution V11
-- ============================================

-- Enable UUID extension
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";

-- ============================================
-- DOMÍNIOS E TIPOS CUSTOMIZADOS
-- ============================================

CREATE DOMAIN email_domain AS VARCHAR(255)
CHECK (VALUE ~ '^[A-Za-z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+\.[A-Za-z]{2,}$');

CREATE DOMAIN phone_domain AS VARCHAR(20)
CHECK (VALUE ~ '^\+?[1-9]\d{1,14}$');

CREATE DOMAIN status_domain AS VARCHAR(50)
CHECK (VALUE IN ('active', 'inactive', 'pending', 'suspended', 'deleted'));

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: users (Camada Raw)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE raw_users (
    user_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    external_id VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE,
    email email_domain NOT NULL,
    phone phone_domain,
    full_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    hashed_password VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    salt VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    status status_domain DEFAULT 'pending',
    email_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    phone_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    two_factor_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    last_login_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    failed_login_attempts INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    locked_until TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Índices
    INDEX idx_raw_users_email ON raw_users(email),
    INDEX idx_raw_users_status ON raw_users(status),
    INDEX idx_raw_users_created_at ON raw_users(created_at),
    INDEX idx_raw_users_metadata ON raw_users USING GIN(metadata)
);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: user_profiles (Camada Staging)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE stg_user_profiles (
    profile_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES raw_users(user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    avatar_url VARCHAR(500),
    bio TEXT,
    company VARCHAR(255),
    job_title VARCHAR(255),
    location VARCHAR(255),
    website VARCHAR(500),
    social_links JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    preferences JSONB DEFAULT '{
        "notifications": {
            "email": true,
            "push": true,
            "sms": false
        },
        "privacy": {
            "profile_public": true,
            "show_email": false
        },
        "theme": "light"
    }',
    language VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT 'en',
    timezone VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'UTC',
    last_active_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Índices
    INDEX idx_stg_user_profiles_user_id ON stg_user_profiles(user_id),
    INDEX idx_stg_user_profiles_last_active ON stg_user_profiles(last_active_at),
    INDEX idx_stg_user_profiles_preferences ON stg_user_profiles USING GIN(preferences)
);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: projects (Camada Raw)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE raw_projects (
    project_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    external_id VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE,
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES raw_users(user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    title VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
    slug VARCHAR(500) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    category VARCHAR(100),
    difficulty_level VARCHAR(50) CHECK (difficulty_level IN ('beginner', 'intermediate', 'advanced', 'expert')),
    estimated_hours DECIMAL(5,2),
    estimated_cost DECIMAL(10,2),
    status status_domain DEFAULT 'active',
    visibility VARCHAR(50) CHECK (visibility IN ('public', 'private', 'unlisted')) DEFAULT 'public',
    featured BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    tags VARCHAR(255)[] DEFAULT '{}',
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    version INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
    published_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Índices
    INDEX idx_raw_projects_user_id ON raw_projects(user_id),
    INDEX idx_raw_projects_slug ON raw_projects(slug),
    INDEX idx_raw_projects_status ON raw_projects(status),
    INDEX idx_raw_projects_category ON raw_projects(category),
    INDEX idx_raw_projects_tags ON raw_projects USING GIN(tags),
    INDEX idx_raw_projects_created_at ON raw_projects(created_at),
    INDEX idx_raw_projects_featured ON raw_projects(featured) WHERE featured = true
);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: project_steps (Camada Staging)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE stg_project_steps (
    step_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES raw_projects(project_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    step_number INTEGER NOT NULL,
    title VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    content JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}',
    estimated_minutes INTEGER,
    difficulty_adjustment DECIMAL(3,2) DEFAULT 1.0,
    media_urls VARCHAR(500)[] DEFAULT '{}',
    tools_required VARCHAR(255)[] DEFAULT '{}',
    materials_required VARCHAR(255)[] DEFAULT '{}',
    safety_warnings TEXT[] DEFAULT '{}',
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Constraints
    UNIQUE(project_id, step_number),
    CHECK (step_number > 0),
    CHECK (difficulty_adjustment BETWEEN 0.1 AND 5.0),
    
    -- Índices
    INDEX idx_stg_project_steps_project_id ON stg_project_steps(project_id),
    INDEX idx_stg_project_steps_step_number ON stg_project_steps(step_number),
    INDEX idx_stg_project_steps_media_urls ON stg_project_steps USING GIN(media_urls)
);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: llm_interactions (Camada Raw - Dados de IA)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE raw_llm_interactions (
    interaction_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES raw_users(user_id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    project_id UUID REFERENCES raw_projects(project_id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    session_id UUID NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL CHECK (provider IN ('openai', 'anthropic', 'google', 'azure', 'local')),
    model VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    prompt_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    completion_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    total_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6),
    latency_ms INTEGER,
    success BOOLEAN NOT NULL,
    error_message TEXT,
    request_metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    response_metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Índices para queries de custo e performance
    INDEX idx_raw_llm_user_id ON raw_llm_interactions(user_id),
    INDEX idx_raw_llm_project_id ON raw_llm_interactions(project_id),
    INDEX idx_raw_llm_provider_model ON raw_llm_interactions(provider, model),
    INDEX idx_raw_llm_created_at ON raw_llm_interactions(created_at),
    INDEX idx_raw_llm_success ON raw_llm_interactions(success),
    INDEX idx_raw_llm_cost ON raw_llm_interactions(cost_usd)
);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: user_activities (Camada Raw - Eventos)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE raw_user_activities (
    activity_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES raw_users(user_id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    session_id UUID NOT NULL,
    activity_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    entity_type VARCHAR(100),
    entity_id UUID,
    details JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    ip_address INET,
    user_agent TEXT,
    device_info JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    location_info JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Índices
    INDEX idx_raw_activities_user_id ON raw_user_activities(user_id),
    INDEX idx_raw_activities_type ON raw_user_activities(activity_type),
    INDEX idx_raw_activities_created_at ON raw_user_activities(created_at),
    INDEX idx_raw_activities_entity ON raw_user_activities(entity_type, entity_id),
    INDEX idx_raw_activities_details ON raw_user_activities USING GIN(details)
);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: project_metrics (Camada Mart - Métricas de Produto)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE mart_project_metrics (
    metric_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES raw_projects(project_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Engajamento
    views INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    unique_visitors INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    saves INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    shares INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    comments_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Completude
    starts INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    completions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    avg_completion_percentage DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 0,
    avg_time_spent_minutes DECIMAL(8,2) DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Avaliação
    avg_rating DECIMAL(3,2),
    rating_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    difficulty_feedback JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    
    -- Custo (derivado de LLM)
    llm_cost_total DECIMAL(10,6) DEFAULT 0,
    llm_interactions_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Métricas calculadas
    completion_rate DECIMAL(5,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        CASE WHEN starts > 0 THEN (completions::DECIMAL / starts) * 100 ELSE 0 END
    ) STORED,
    engagement_score DECIMAL(5,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        (views * 0.1) + (saves * 0.3) + (shares * 0.5) + (completions * 1.0)
    ) STORED,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Constraints
    UNIQUE(project_id, date),
    CHECK (views >= 0),
    CHECK (completions <= starts),
    CHECK (avg_rating BETWEEN 0 AND 5 OR avg_rating IS NULL),
    
    -- Índices
    INDEX idx_mart_project_metrics_project_date ON mart_project_metrics(project_id, date),
    INDEX idx_mart_project_metrics_date ON mart_project_metrics(date),
    INDEX idx_mart_project_metrics_engagement ON mart_project_metrics(engagement_score DESC),
    INDEX idx_mart_project_metrics_completion_rate ON mart_project_metrics(completion_rate DESC)
);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: user_metrics (Camada Mart - Métricas de Usuário)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE mart_user_metrics (
    metric_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES raw_users(user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Atividade
    sessions_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_time_minutes DECIMAL(8,2) DEFAULT 0,
    projects_viewed INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    projects_started INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    projects_completed INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Criação
    projects_created INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    steps_created INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    comments_posted INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Engajamento com IA
    llm_interactions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    llm_cost_total DECIMAL(10,6) DEFAULT 0,
    avg_llm_latency_ms DECIMAL(8,2),
    
    -- Retenção
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    streak_days INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Métricas calculadas
    daily_active_minutes DECIMAL(8,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        CASE WHEN sessions_count > 0 THEN total_time_minutes / sessions_count ELSE 0 END
    ) STORED,
    completion_rate DECIMAL(5,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        CASE WHEN projects_started > 0 THEN (projects_completed::DECIMAL / projects_started) * 100 ELSE 0 END
    ) STORED,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Constraints
    UNIQUE(user_id, date),
    
    -- Índices
    INDEX idx_mart_user_metrics_user_date ON mart_user_metrics(user_id, date),
    INDEX idx_mart_user_metrics_date ON mart_user_metrics(date),
    INDEX idx_mart_user_metrics_active ON mart_user_metrics(is_active),
    INDEX idx_mart_user_metrics_streak ON mart_user_metrics(streak_days DESC)
);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: llm_cost_metrics (Camada Mart - Custo de IA)
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE mart_llm_cost_metrics (
    metric_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    hour INTEGER CHECK (hour BETWEEN 0 AND 23),
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    model VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    feature VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Volume
    request_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    success_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    error_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Tokens
    total_prompt_tokens BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    total_completion_tokens BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    total_tokens BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Custo
    total_cost_usd DECIMAL(12,6) DEFAULT 0,
    avg_cost_per_request DECIMAL(10,6),
    
    -- Performance
    avg_latency_ms DECIMAL(8,2),
    p95_latency_ms DECIMAL(8,2),
    p99_latency_ms DECIMAL(8,2),
    
    -- Métricas calculadas
    success_rate DECIMAL(5,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        CASE WHEN request_count > 0 THEN (success_count::DECIMAL / request_count) * 100 ELSE 0 END
    ) STORED,
    tokens_per_request DECIMAL(8,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        CASE WHEN request_count > 0 THEN total_tokens::DECIMAL / request_count ELSE 0 END
    ) STORED,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Constraints
    UNIQUE(date, hour, provider, model, feature),
    
    -- Índices
    INDEX idx_mart_llm_cost_date ON mart_llm_cost_metrics(date),
    INDEX idx_mart_llm_cost_provider_model ON mart_llm_cost_metrics(provider, model),
    INDEX idx_mart_llm_cost_feature ON mart_llm_cost_metrics(feature),
    INDEX idx_mart_llm_cost_total ON mart_llm_cost_metrics(total_cost_usd DESC)
);

-- ============================================
-- FUNÇÕES E TRIGGERS
-- ============================================

-- Função para atualizar updated_at automaticamente
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    NEW.updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP;
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

-- Triggers para updated_at
CREATE TRIGGER update_raw_users_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON raw_users 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_stg_user_profiles_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON stg_user_profiles 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_raw_projects_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON raw_projects 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_stg_project_steps_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON stg_project_steps 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_mart_project_metrics_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON mart_project_metrics 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_mart_user_metrics_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON mart_user_metrics 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_mart_llm_cost_metrics_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON mart_llm_cost_metrics 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

-- Função para soft delete
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION soft_delete_record()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    NEW.deleted_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP;
    NEW.status = 'deleted';
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

-- Função para gerar slug automático
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION generate_slug(title VARCHAR, id UUID)
RETURNS VARCHAR AS $$
DECL

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Camada de Segurança

Vou implementar uma camada de segurança completa com autenticação JWT, sanitização de inputs, rate limiting, CORS configurado e validação de dados em todas as camadas. Vou estruturar isso como um middleware de segurança modular que pode ser facilmente integrado ao sistema existente.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
security-layer/
├── src/
│   ├── middleware/
│   │   ├── auth.js
│   │   ├── sanitize.js
│   │   ├── rateLimit.js
│   │   ├── cors.js
│   │   ├── validation.js
│   │   └── security.js
│   ├── utils/
│   │   ├── jwt.js
│   │   ├── validator.js
│   │   ├── sanitizer.js
│   │   └── securityLogger.js
│   ├── models/
│   │   └── User.js
│   ├── controllers/
│   │   └── authController.js
│   ├── routes/
│   │   └── authRoutes.js
│   └── config/
│       └── securityConfig.js
├── public/
│   ├── index.html
│   └── dashboard.js
├── tests/
│   └── security.test.js
├── package.json
└── README.md

## 1. Configuração de Segurança (securityConfig.js)

```javascript
// src/config/securityConfig.js
const securityConfig = {
  // JWT Configuration
  jwt: {
    secret: process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your-super-secret-jwt-key-change-in-production',
    accessTokenExpiry: '15m',
    refreshTokenExpiry: '7d',
    issuer: 'diyapp-v11',
    audience: 'diyapp-users'
  },
  
  // Rate Limiting Configuration
  rateLimit: {
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 100, // Limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
    message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again later.',
    skipSuccessfulRequests: false
  },
  
  // CORS Configuration
  cors: {
    origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS.split(',') : ['http://localhost:3000'],
    methods: ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'PATCH'],
    allowedHeaders: ['Content-Type', 'Authorization', 'X-Requested-With'],
    exposedHeaders: ['X-RateLimit-Limit', 'X-RateLimit-Remaining'],
    credentials: true,
    maxAge: 86400 // 24 hours
  },
  
  // Input Validation Rules
  validation: {
    username: {
      min: 3,
      max: 30,
      pattern: /^[a-zA-Z0-9_]+$/,
      message: 'Username must be 3-30 characters, alphanumeric and underscores only'
    },
    password: {
      min: 8,
      max: 100,
      requireUppercase: true,
      requireLowercase: true,
      requireNumbers: true,
      requireSpecialChars: true,
      message: 'Password must be 8-100 characters with uppercase, lowercase, number and special character'
    },
    email: {
      pattern: /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/,
      message: 'Please provide a valid email address'
    }
  },
  
  // Security Headers
  headers: {
    contentSecurityPolicy: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'", "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'", "https://fonts.googleapis.com"],
      fontSrc: ["'self'", "https://fonts.gstatic.com"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      frameSrc: ["'none'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"]
    },
    hsts: {
      maxAge: 31536000, // 1 year
      includeSubDomains: true,
      preload: true
    }
  }
};

module.exports = securityConfig;
```

## 2. Utilitário JWT (jwt.js)

```javascript
// src/utils/jwt.js
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const securityConfig = require('../config/securityConfig');

class JWTManager {
  constructor() {
    this.secret = securityConfig.jwt.secret;
    this.accessTokenExpiry = securityConfig.jwt.accessTokenExpiry;
    this.refreshTokenExpiry = securityConfig.jwt.refreshTokenExpiry;
  }

  // Generate access token
  generateAccessToken(user) {
    const payload = {
      sub: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      role: user.role,
      iat: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000),
      iss: securityConfig.jwt.issuer,
      aud: securityConfig.jwt.audience,
      type: 'access'
    };

    return jwt.sign(payload, this.secret, {
      expiresIn: this.accessTokenExpiry
    });
  }

  // Generate refresh token
  generateRefreshToken(user) {
    const payload = {
      sub: user.id,
      type: 'refresh',
      iat: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000),
      iss: securityConfig.jwt.issuer,
      aud: securityConfig.jwt.audience
    };

    return jwt.sign(payload, this.secret, {
      expiresIn: this.refreshTokenExpiry
    });
  }

  // Verify token
  verifyToken(token) {
    try {
      return jwt.verify(token, this.secret, {
        issuer: securityConfig.jwt.issuer,
        audience: securityConfig.jwt.audience
      });
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(`Token verification failed: ${error.message}`);
    }
  }

  // Decode token without verification (for logging purposes only)
  decodeToken(token) {
    return jwt.decode(token);
  }

  // Generate secure random string for tokens
  generateSecureRandom(length = 32) {
    return crypto.randomBytes(length).toString('hex');
  }

  // Check if token is about to expire (for proactive refresh)
  isTokenExpiringSoon(token, thresholdMinutes = 5) {
    try {
      const decoded = this.verifyToken(token);
      const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
      const timeLeft = decoded.exp - now;
      return timeLeft < (thresholdMinutes * 60);
    } catch (error) {
      return true;
    }
  }
}

module.exports = new JWTManager();
```

## 3. Sanitizador de Inputs (sanitizer.js)

```javascript
// src/utils/sanitizer.js
const DOMPurify = require('isomorphic-dompurify');
const validator = require('validator');

class InputSanitizer {
  constructor() {
    // Configure DOMPurify
    DOMPurify.setConfig({
      ALLOWED_TAGS: ['b', 'i', 'em', 'strong', 'a', 'p', 'br', 'ul', 'ol', 'li'],
      ALLOWED_ATTR: ['href', 'target', 'rel'],
      ALLOW_DATA_ATTR: false
    });
  }

  // Sanitize HTML input
  sanitizeHTML(input) {
    if (typeof input !== 'string') return input;
    return DOMPurify.sanitize(input);
  }

  // Sanitize for SQL injection prevention
  sanitizeSQL(input) {
    if (typeof input !== 'string') return input;
    
    // Remove common SQL injection patterns
    const sqlInjectionPatterns = [
      /(\b(SELECT|INSERT|UPDATE|DELETE|DROP|UNION|EXEC|ALTER|CREATE|TRUNCATE)\b)/gi,
      /(\b(OR|AND)\b\s*\d+\s*=\s*\d+)/gi,
      /(--|\/\*|\*\/|;)/g,
      /(\b(WAITFOR|DELAY)\b.*)/gi
    ];

    let sanitized = input;
    sqlInjectionPatterns.forEach(pattern => {
      sanitized = sanitized.replace(pattern, '');
    });

    return sanitized.trim();
  }

  // Sanitize for XSS prevention
  sanitizeXSS(input) {
    if (typeof input !== 'string') return input;
    
    // Remove script tags and event handlers
    const xssPatterns = [
      /<script\b[^<]*(?:(?!<\/script>)<[^<]*)*<\/script>/gi,
      /javascript:/gi,
      /on\w+\s*=/gi,
      /data:/gi,
      /vbscript:/gi
    ];

    let sanitized = input;
    xssPatterns.forEach(pattern => {
      sanitized = sanitized.replace(pattern, '');
    });

    return this.sanitizeHTML(sanitized);
  }

  // Sanitize file paths
  sanitizeFilePath(input) {
    if (typeof input !== 'string') return input;
    
    // Remove directory traversal attempts
    const traversalPatterns = [
      /\.\.\//g,
      /\.\.\\/g,
      /\/\/+/g,
      /\\+/g
    ];

    let sanitized = input;
    traversalPatterns.forEach(pattern => {
      sanitized = sanitized.replace(pattern, '');
    });

    // Remove null bytes
    sanitized = sanitized.replace(/\0/g, '');
    
    return sanitized;
  }

  // Sanitize email
  sanitizeEmail(email) {
    if (typeof email !== 'string') return '';
    const sanitized = validator.normalizeEmail(email.trim());
    return validator.isEmail(sanitized) ? sanitized : '';
  }

  // Sanitize URL
  sanitizeURL(url) {
    if (typeof url !== 'string') return '';
    const sanitized = url.trim();
    return validator.isURL(sanitized) ? sanitized : '';
  }

  // Sanitize phone number
  sanitizePhone(phone) {
    if (typeof phone !== 'string') return '';
    const sanitized = phone.replace(/[^\d+]/g, '');
    return validator.isMobilePhone(sanitized, 'any') ? sanitized : '';
  }

  // Deep sanitize object
  deepSanitize(obj, options = {}) {
    if (!obj || typeof obj !== 'object') return obj;

    const sanitized = Array.isArray(obj) ? [] : {};
    const {
      sanitizeHTML: doHTML = true,
      sanitizeSQL: doSQL = true,
      sanitizeXSS: doXSS = true,
      allowedFields = null
    } = options;

    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(obj)) {
      // Skip if field not in allowedFields list
      if (allowedFields && !allowedFields.includes(key)) {
        continue;
      }

      if (typeof value === 'string') {
        let sanitizedValue = value;
        
        if (doSQL) sanitizedValue = this.sanitizeSQL(sanitizedValue);
        if (doXSS) sanitizedValue = this.sanitizeXSS(sanitizedValue);
        if (doHTML) sanitizedValue = this.sanitizeHTML(sanitizedValue);
        
        sanitized[key] = sanitizedValue;
      } else if (typeof value === 'object' && value !== null) {
        sanitized[key] = this.deepSanitize(value, options);
      } else {
        sanitized[key] = value;
      }
    }

    return sanitized;
  }
}

module.exports = new InputSanitizer();
```

## 4. Validador de Dados (validator.js)

```javascript
// src/utils/validator.js
const validator = require('validator');
const securityConfig = require('../config/securityConfig');

class DataValidator {
  constructor() {
    this.rules = securityConfig.validation;
  }

  // Validate username
  validateUsername(username) {
    const { min, max, pattern } = this.rules.username;
    
    if (typeof username !== 'string') {
      return { isValid: false, message: 'Username must be a string' };
    }

    const trimmed = username.trim();
    
    if (trimmed.length < min || trimmed.length > max) {
      return { 
        isValid: false, 
        message: `Username must be between ${min} and ${max} characters` 
      };
    }

    if (!pattern.test(trimmed)) {
      return { 
        isValid: false, 
        message: this.rules.username.message 
      };
    }

    return { isValid: true, value: trimmed };
  }

  // Validate password strength
  validatePassword(password) {
    const { 
      min, 
      max, 
      requireUppercase, 
      requireLowercase, 
      requireNumbers, 
      requireSpecialChars 
    } = this.rules.password;

    if (typeof password !== 'string') {
      return { isValid: false, message: 'Password must be a string' };
    }

    if (password.length < min || password.length > max) {
      return { 
        isValid: false, 
        message: `Password must be between ${min} and ${max} characters` 
      };
    }

    const errors = [];
    
    if (requireUppercase && !/[A-Z]/.test(password)) {
      errors.push('at least one uppercase letter');
    }
    
    if (requireLowercase && !/[a-z]/.test(password)) {
      errors.push('at least one lowercase letter');
    }
    
    if (requireNumbers && !/\d/.test(password)) {
      errors.push('at least one number');
    }
    
    if (requireSpecialChars && !/[!@#$%^&*()_+\-=\[\]{};':"\\|,.<>\/?]/.test(password)) {
      errors.push('at least one special character');
    }

    if (errors.length > 0) {
      return { 
        isValid: false, 
        message: `Password must contain ${errors.join(', ')}` 
      };
    }

    return { isValid: true, value: password };
  }

  // Validate email
  validateEmail(email) {
    if (typeof email !== 'string') {
      return { isValid: false, message: 'Email must be a string' };
    }

    const trimmed = email.trim().toLowerCase();
    
    if (!validator.isEmail(trimmed)) {
      return { isValid: false, message: this.rules.email.message };
    }

    // Additional email validation
    if (!validator.isLength(trimmed, { max: 254 })) {
      return { isValid: false, message: 'Email is too long' };
    }

    return { isValid: true, value: trimmed };
  }

  // Validate input against schema
  validateSchema(data, schema) {
    const errors = {};
    const sanitizedData = {};

    for (const [field, rules] of Object.entries(schema)) {
      const value = data[field];
      const isRequired = rules.required !== false;
      
      // Check if required field is missing
      if (isRequired && (value === undefined || value === null || value === '')) {
        errors[field] = `${field} is required`;
        continue;
      }

      // Skip validation if field is optional and empty
      if (!isRequired && (value === undefined || value === null || value === '')) {
        sanitizedData[field] = value;
        continue;
      }

      // Type validation
      if (rules.type) {
        if (rules.type === 'string' && typeof value !== 'string') {
          errors[field] = `${field} must be a string`;
          continue;
        }
        if (rules.type === 'number' && typeof value !== 'number') {
          errors[field] = `${field} must be a number`;
          continue;
        }
        if (rules.type === 'boolean' && typeof value !== 'boolean') {
          errors[field] = `${field} must be a boolean`;
          continue;
        }
        if (rules.type === 'array' && !Array.isArray(value)) {
          errors[field] = `${field} must be an array`;
          continue;
        }
        if (rules.type === 'object' && (typeof value !== 'object' || Array.isArray(value))) {
          errors[field] = `${field} must be an object`;
          continue;
        }
      }

      // String validations
      if (rules.type === 'string' || typeof value === 'string') {
        const stringValue = String(value);
        
        if (rules.minLength && stringValue.length < rules.minLength) {
          errors[field] = `${field} must be at least ${rules.minLength} characters`;
          continue;
        }
        
        if (rules.maxLength && stringValue.length > rules.maxLength) {
          errors[field] = `${field} must be at most ${rules.maxLength} characters`;
          continue;
        }
        
        if (rules.pattern && !rules.pattern.test(stringValue)) {
          errors[field] = rules.message || `${field} format is invalid`;
          continue;
        }
        
        if (rules.enum && !rules.enum.includes(stringValue)) {
          errors[field] = `${field} must be one of: ${rules.enum.join(', ')}`;
          continue;
        }

        sanitizedData[field] = stringValue;
      } else {
        sanitizedData[field] = value;
      }
    }

    return {
      isValid: Object.keys(errors).length === 0,
      errors,
      data: sanitizedData
    };
  }

  // Validate API input with common schemas
  validateAPIInput(data, endpoint) {
    const schemas = {
      register: {
        username: { type: 'string', required: true, minLength: 3, maxLength: 30 },
        email: { type: 'string', required: true, pattern: /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/ },
        password: { type: 'string', required: true, minLength: 8 }
      },
      login: {
        email: { type: 'string', required: true },
        password: { type: 'string', required: true }
      },
      updateProfile: {
        username: { type: 'string', required: false, min

### [Sessão Paralela: QA]

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-core/
├── src/

│   └── index.js

## 2. Critérios de Aceite Gherkin

### features/chat_functionality.feature
```gherkin
Feature: Chat Interface Functionality
  As a user
  I want to interact with the AI assistant
  So that I can get helpful responses to my queries

  Background:
    Given the chat interface is loaded
    And I am authenticated as a valid user

  Scenario: Send message and receive response
    Given I have entered a valid message "Hello, how are you?"
    When I click the send button
    Then I should see my message in the chat history
    And I should see a response from the AI within 5 seconds
    And the response should be non-empty and relevant to my query

  Scenario: Handle empty message
    Given I have not entered any message
    When I click the send button
    Then I should see an error message "Message cannot be empty"
    And the send button should be disabled

  Scenario: Handle long messages
    Given I have entered a message longer than 5000 characters
    When I click the send button
    Then I should see an error message "Message is too long"
    And the message should be truncated to 5000 characters

  Scenario: Clear chat history
    Given I have sent at least one message
    And I have received a response
    When I click the clear chat button
    Then the chat history should be empty
    And I should see a confirmation message

  Scenario: Save chat conversation
    Given I have a conversation with at least 3 messages
    When I click the save conversation button
    Then the conversation should be saved to my history
    And I should receive a success notification
    And I should be able to retrieve it later

  Scenario: Handle network error
    Given the API server is unavailable
    When I send a message
    Then I should see an error message "Unable to connect to server"
    And I should have an option to retry
    And the retry button should be enabled
```

### features/llm_validation.feature
```gherkin
Feature: LLM Output Validation
  As a QA engineer
  I want to validate LLM outputs
  So that we maintain consistent quality and prevent regression

  Background:
    Given I have access to the LLM validation dashboard
    And the golden dataset is loaded

  Scenario: Validate golden dataset prompts
    Given I have a set of 50 golden prompts
    When I run the validation suite
    Then all prompts should return responses
    And at least 95% of responses should match expected patterns
    And no response should contain prohibited content
    And response time should be under 2 seconds per prompt

  Scenario: Detect output drift
    Given I have baseline metrics from the previous model version
    When I run the same prompts on the new model
    Then the similarity score should be at least 90%
    And the quality score should not degrade by more than 10%
    If degradation exceeds 10%
    Then the deployment should be blocked
    And an alert should be sent to the AI Ops team

  Scenario: Test adversarial inputs
    Given I have a set of adversarial prompts
    When I submit these prompts to the LLM
    Then all responses should be safely handled
    And no system information should be leaked
    And the system should not crash
    And inappropriate content should be filtered

  Scenario: Test consistency across multiple runs
    Given the same prompt with temperature 0.2
    When I run it 10 times
    Then the responses should be semantically similar
    And the variance score should be below 0.1
    And the exact match rate should be at least 80%

  Scenario: Test guardrails effectiveness
    Given prompts attempting prompt injection
    When I submit these prompts
    Then the system should reject them
    Or sanitize the output appropriately
    And log the attempt for security review
```

### features/user_authentication.feature
```gherkin
Feature: User Authentication
  As a user
  I want to securely authenticate
  So that I can access my personalized features

  Scenario: Successful login with valid credentials
    Given I am on the login page
    When I enter valid credentials
    And I click the login button
    Then I should be redirected to the dashboard
    And I should see my username displayed
    And a session token should be created

  Scenario: Failed login with invalid credentials
    Given I am on the login page
    When I enter invalid credentials
    And I click the login button
    Then I should see an error message
    And I should remain on the login page
    And no session should be created

  Scenario: Logout functionality
    Given I am logged in
    When I click the logout button
    Then I should be redirected to the login page
    And my session should be destroyed
    And I should not be able to access protected routes

  Scenario: Session timeout
    Given I am logged in
    When I remain inactive for 30 minutes
    Then my session should expire
    And I should be redirected to the login page
    And I should see a session expired message

  Scenario: Password reset flow
    Given I am on the password reset page
    When I enter my registered email
    And I click the reset button
    Then I should receive a reset email
    And I should be able to set a new password
    And the new password should work for login
```

## 3. Testes Unitários

### src/components/Button/Button.test.jsx
```javascript
import React from 'react';
import { render, screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react';
import '@testing-library/jest-dom';
import Button from './Button';

describe('Button Component', () => {
  test('renders button with correct text', () => {
    render(<Button label="Click me" />);
    expect(screen.getByRole('button', { name: /click me/i })).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  test('calls onClick handler when clicked', () => {
    const handleClick = jest.fn();
    render(<Button label="Click" onClick={handleClick} />);
    fireEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button'));
    expect(handleClick).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
  });

  test('is disabled when disabled prop is true', () => {
    render(<Button label="Disabled" disabled={true} />);
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toBeDisabled();
  });

  test('shows loading state when loading prop is true', () => {
    render(<Button label="Loading" loading={true} />);
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveAttribute('aria-busy', 'true');
    expect(screen.getByText('Loading...')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  test('applies correct CSS classes based on variant', () => {
    const { rerender } = render(<Button label="Primary" variant="primary" />);
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveClass('btn-primary');
    
    rerender(<Button label="Secondary" variant="secondary" />);
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveClass('btn-secondary');
  });

  test('handles keyboard navigation', () => {
    const handleClick = jest.fn();
    render(<Button label="Enter" onClick={handleClick} />);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    
    fireEvent.keyDown(button, { key: 'Enter', code: 'Enter' });
    expect(handleClick).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
    
    fireEvent.keyDown(button, { key: ' ', code: 'Space' });
    expect(handleClick).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(2);
  });
});
```

### src/services/llmService.test.js
```javascript
const llmService = require('./llmService');
const { validateLLMOutput, detectContentViolation } = require('../utils/validation');

jest.mock('../utils/validation');

describe('LLM Service', () => {
  let mockOpenAI;
  
  beforeEach(() => {
    mockOpenAI = {
      chat: {
        completions: {
          create: jest.fn()
        }
      }
    };
    
    llmService.setClient(mockOpenAI);
    validateLLMOutput.mockClear();
    detectContentViolation.mockClear();
  });

  describe('generateResponse', () => {
    test('returns valid response for normal prompt', async () => {
      const mockResponse = {
        choices: [{
          message: {
            content: 'This is a helpful response.',
            role: 'assistant'
          }
        }]
      };
      
      mockOpenAI.chat.completions.create.mockResolvedValue(mockResponse);
      validateLLMOutput.mockReturnValue({ isValid: true, score: 0.95 });
      detectContentViolation.mockReturnValue({ hasViolation: false });
      
      const result = await llmService.generateResponse('Hello', { temperature: 0.7 });
      
      expect(result.success).toBe(true);
      expect(result.content).toBe('This is a helpful response.');
      expect(result.metadata.score).toBe(0.95);
      expect(mockOpenAI.chat.completions.create).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.objectContaining({
          messages: expect.arrayContaining([
            expect.objectContaining({ role: 'user', content: 'Hello' })
          ]),
          temperature: 0.7
        })
      );
    });

    test('handles empty prompt', async () => {
      const result = await llmService.generateResponse('');
      expect(result.success).toBe(false);
      expect(result.error).toBe('Prompt cannot be empty');
    });

    test('handles prompt too long', async () => {
      const longPrompt = 'A'.repeat(10001);
      const result = await llmService.generateResponse(longPrompt);
      expect(result.success).toBe(false);
      expect(result.error).toContain('too long');
    });

    test('detects and handles content violations', async () => {
      const mockResponse = {
        choices: [{
          message: {
            content: 'Inappropriate content here',
            role: 'assistant'
          }
        }]
      };
      
      mockOpenAI.chat.completions.create.mockResolvedValue(mockResponse);
      detectContentViolation.mockReturnValue({
        hasViolation: true,
        violationType: 'prohibited_content',
        filteredContent: 'Content filtered due to policy violation'
      });
      
      const result = await llmService.generateResponse('bad prompt');
      
      expect(result.success).toBe(false);
      expect(result.content).toBe('Content filtered due to policy violation');
      expect(result.metadata.filtered).toBe(true);
    });

    test('handles API errors gracefully', async () => {
      mockOpenAI.chat.completions.create.mockRejectedValue(
        new Error('API rate limit exceeded')
      );
      
      const result = await llmService.generateResponse('test');
      
      expect(result.success).toBe(false);
      expect(result.error).toContain('rate limit');
      expect(result.retryable).toBe(true);
    });

    test('measures response time', async () => {
      mockOpenAI.chat.completions.create.mockImplementation(() => {
        return new Promise(resolve => {
          setTimeout(() => resolve({
            choices: [{ message: { content: 'Response', role: 'assistant' } }]
          }), 100);
        });
      });
      
      const startTime = Date.now();
      const result = await llmService.generateResponse('test');
      const endTime = Date.now();
      
      expect(result.success).toBe(true);
      expect(result.metadata.responseTime).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(100);
      expect(result.metadata.responseTime).toBeLessThan(200);
    });
  });

  describe('batchProcess', () => {
    test('processes multiple prompts in batch', async () => {
      const prompts = ['Prompt 1', 'Prompt 2', 'Prompt 3'];
      const mockResponse = {
        choices: [{ message: { content: 'Response', role: 'assistant' } }]
      };
      
      mockOpenAI.chat.completions.create.mockRes

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Writer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Documentação Técnica

## 📋 Visão Geral

DIYAPP Evolution V11 é uma plataforma autônoma de fábrica de software que integra múltiplos agentes de IA especializados em uma squad de desenvolvimento colaborativo. O sistema permite desenvolvimento recursivo, onde os próprios agentes podem evoluir o código-base da aplicação.

## 🚀 Setup Rápido

### Pré-requisitos
```bash
# Node.js 18+ e npm
node --version
npm --version

# Python 3.9+ (para alguns agentes)
python --version

# Git
git --version

# Docker e Docker Compose (opcional, para containerização)
docker --version
docker-compose --version
```

### Instalação Local

1. **Clone o repositório**
```bash
git clone https://github.com/diyapp/evolution-v11-core.git
cd evolution-v11-core
```

2. **Instale dependências**
```bash
# Instalar dependências principais
npm install

# Instalar dependências de desenvolvimento
npm install -D typescript @types/node ts-node nodemon

# Instalar agentes especializados
npm install @diyapp/agent-dev-backend @diyapp/agent-dev-frontend @diyapp/agent-tech-lead
```

3. **Configure variáveis de ambiente**
```bash
cp .env.example .env
# Edite .env com suas configurações
```

4. **Inicie o sistema**
```bash
# Modo desenvolvimento
npm run dev

# Modo produção
npm start

# Modo Hive (refatoração paralela)
npm run hive
```

### Docker Compose (Recomendado)

```yaml
# docker-compose.yml
version: '3.8'
services:
  diyapp-core:
    build: .
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
      - "3001:3001"  # Swagger UI
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - OPENAI_API_KEY=${OPENAI_API_KEY}
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://postgres:password@db:5432/diyapp
    depends_on:
      - db
      - redis
  
  db:
    image: postgres:15
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_DB=diyapp
      - POSTGRES_USER=postgres
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=password
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
  
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
  
  swagger-ui:
    image: swaggerapi/swagger-ui
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    environment:
      - SWAGGER_JSON=/api/openapi.json
    volumes:
      - ./docs/openapi.json:/api/openapi.json

volumes:
  postgres_data:
```

```bash
# Iniciar com Docker Compose
docker-compose up -d

# Verificar logs
docker-compose logs -f diyapp-core
```

## 📚 Documentação da API

### Acesso à Documentação Interativa

1. **Swagger UI**: http://localhost:3001/api-docs
2. **OpenAPI JSON**: http://localhost:3000/api/openapi.json
3. **ReDoc**: http://localhost:3000/api/redoc

### Endpoints Principais

#### 1. API de Agentes

```http
GET /api/v1/agents
```
**Descrição**: Lista todos os agentes disponíveis no sistema

**Resposta**:
```json
{
  "agents": [
    {
      "id": "dev-backend",
      "name": "Dev Backend",
      "status": "active",
      "capabilities": ["api-development", "database-design"],
      "version": "2.1.0"
    }
  ],
  "total": 8,
  "active": 8
}
```

#### 2. API de Tarefas

```http
POST /api/v1/tasks
```
**Descrição**: Cria uma nova tarefa para a squad

**Corpo da Requisição**:
```json
{
  "title": "Implementar autenticação JWT",
  "description": "Adicionar sistema de autenticação com tokens JWT",
  "priority": "high",
  "assignedAgent": "dev-backend",
  "dependencies": ["database-setup"]
}
```

**Resposta**:
```json
{
  "taskId": "task_abc123",
  "status": "queued",
  "estimatedCompletion": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",
  "assignedTo": "dev-backend",
  "monitorUrl": "/api/v1/tasks/task_abc123/status"
}
```

#### 3. API de Código

```http
POST /api/v1/code/analyze
```
**Descrição**: Analisa e sugere melhorias no código

**Corpo da Requisição**:
```json
{
  "code": "function example() { return 'test'; }",
  "language": "javascript",
  "analysisType": "quality"
}
```

#### 4. API de Modo Hive

```http
POST /api/v1/hive/refactor
```
**Descrição**: Inicia refatoração paralela usando Modo Hive

**Parâmetros de Query**:
- `strategy`: "parallel" | "sequential" | "rolling"
- `maxConcurrent`: número (padrão: 3)
- `safetyCheck`: boolean (padrão: true)

### Autenticação

```http
POST /api/v1/auth/login
```
**Corpo**:
```json
{
  "apiKey": "sua_chave_api",
  "agentId": "seu_agent_id"
}
```

**Resposta**:
```json
{
  "token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9...",
  "expiresIn": 3600,
  "agent": {
    "id": "dev-backend",
    "permissions": ["read", "write", "execute"]
  }
}
```

**Uso do Token**:
```bash
curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <token>" http://localhost:3000/api/v1/agents
```

### Códigos de Erro

| Código | Descrição | Solução |
|--------|-----------|----------|
| 4001 | Agente não encontrado | Verifique o agentId ou registre o agente |
| 4002 | Tarefa já em execução | Aguarde a conclusão ou cancele a tarefa |
| 4003 | Dependência não satisfeita | Complete as tarefas dependentes primeiro |
| 5001 | Erro interno do Modo Hive | Verifique logs e reinicie o serviço |
| 5002 | Timeout de comunicação | Aumente timeout ou verifique conectividade |

## 🏗️ Arquitetura do Sistema

### Estrutura de Diretórios
```
diyapp-evolution-v11-core/
├── src/
│   ├── agents/           # Implementações dos agentes
│   │   ├── dev-backend/
│   │   ├── dev-frontend/
│   │   ├── tech-lead/
│   │   └── tech-writer/
│   ├── core/             # Núcleo do sistema
│   │   ├── orchestrator/ # Orquestrador de tarefas
│   │   ├── communication/# Sistema de comunicação
│   │   └── monitoring/   # Monitoramento e logs
│   ├── api/              # API REST
│   │   ├── controllers/
│   │   ├── routes/
│   │   └── middleware/
│   ├── hive/             # Modo Hive
│   │   ├── strategies/
│   │   ├── safety/
│   │   └── parallelizer/
│   └── utils/            # Utilitários compartilhados
├── public/               # Arquivos estáticos
│   └── index.html        # Dashboard principal
├── tests/                # Testes automatizados
├── docs/                 # Documentação
├── scripts/              # Scripts de automação
└── config/               # Configurações
```

### Diagrama de Componentes
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    Dashboard (index.html)                   │
└──────────────────────────────┬──────────────────────────────┘
                               │
┌──────────────────────────────▼──────────────────────────────┐
│                    API Gateway (Express)                    │
└─────┬────────────────┬────────────────┬─────────────────────┘
      │                │                │
┌─────▼─────┐  ┌──────▼──────┐  ┌──────▼──────┐
│  Agents   │  │   Tasks     │  │    Hive     │
│  Manager  │  │  Orchestrator│  │  Controller │
└─────┬─────┘  └──────┬──────┘  └──────┬──────┘
      │                │                │
┌─────▼────────────────▼────────────────▼─────┐
│          Communication Bus (Redis)          │
└─────┬────────────────┬────────────────┬─────┘
      │                │                │
┌─────▼─────┐  ┌──────▼──────┐  ┌──────▼──────┐
│ Dev Back- │  │ Dev Front-  │  │  Tech Lead  │
│   end     │  │    end      │  │             │
└───────────┘  └─────────────┘  └─────────────┘
```

## 🔧 Guia de Desenvolvimento

### Padrões de Código

#### JavaScript/TypeScript
```javascript
/**
 * @class AgentOrchestrator
 * @description Orquestra a execução de tarefas entre agentes
 * @version 2.1.0
 * 
 * @example
 * const orchestrator = new AgentOrchestrator();
 * await orchestrator.assignTask(task, 'dev-backend');
 */
class AgentOrchestrator {
  /**
   * @param {Object} config - Configuração do orquestrador
   * @param {number} config.maxConcurrentTasks - Máximo de tarefas concorrentes
   * @param {boolean} config.enableHiveMode - Habilita Modo Hive
   */
  constructor(config = {}) {
    this.maxConcurrentTasks = config.maxConcurrentTasks || 5;
    this.enableHiveMode = config.enableHiveMode || false;
    this.activeTasks = new Map();
  }

  /**
   * Atribui uma tarefa a um agente específico
   * @async
   * @param {Task} task - Objeto tarefa a ser executada
   * @param {string} agentId - ID do agente designado
   * @returns {Promise<TaskResult>} Resultado da execução
   * @throws {AgentNotFoundError} Se agente não existir
   * @throws {TaskQueueFullError} Se fila estiver cheia
   */
  async assignTask(task, agentId) {
    // Implementação
  }
}
```

#### Comentários de Documentação
```typescript
/**
 * INTERFACE: Task
 * DESCRIÇÃO: Representa uma tarefa no sistema DIYAPP
 * CONTEXTO: Usado pelo orquestrador para gerenciar execução
 * 
 * @property {string} id - Identificador único (UUID)
 * @property {string} title - Título descritivo da tarefa
 * @property {'high'|'medium'|'low'} priority - Prioridade de execução
 * @property {string[]} dependencies - IDs de tarefas dependentes
 * @property {Date} createdAt - Data de criação
 * @property {AgentID} assignedTo - Agente responsável
 */
interface Task {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  description?: string;
  priority: 'high' | 'medium' | 'low';
  dependencies: string[];
  createdAt: Date;
  assignedTo?: string;
  status: TaskStatus;
}

/**
 * ENUM: TaskStatus
 * DESCRIÇÃO: Estados possíveis de uma tarefa
 * FLUXO: queued → assigned → running → completed/failed
 */
enum TaskStatus {
  QUEUED = 'queued',
  ASSIGNED = 'assigned',
  RUNNING = 'running',
  COMPLETED = 'completed',
  FAILED = 'failed',
  CANCELLED = 'cancelled'
}
```

### Modo Hive - Refatoração Paralela

#### Configuração
```javascript
// config/hive.config.js
module.exports = {
  // Estratégias de refatoração
  strategies: {
    parallel: {
      maxConcurrent: 3,
      timeout: 300000, // 5 minutos
      rollbackOnFailure: true
    },
    sequential: {
      order: 'dependency', // 'dependency' | 'complexity' | 'random'
      validateEachStep: true
    }
  },
  
  // Verificações de segurança
  safety: {
    preCheck: {
      runTests: true,
      checkDependencies: true,
      backupOriginal: true
    },
    postCheck: {
      validateBuild: true,
      runIntegrationTests: true,
      comparePerformance: true
    }
  },
  
  // Monitoramento
  monitoring: {
    logLevel: 'verbose',
    metrics: ['executionTime', 'successRate', 'conflictCount'],
    alertOn: {
      failure: true,
      timeout: true,
      conflict: true
    }
  }
};
```

#### Uso Programático
```javascript
const hive = require('./src/hive/controller');

async function refactorProject() {
  const result = await hive.executeRefactor({
    target: './src/agents',
    strategy: 'parallel',
    options: {
      maxConcurrent: 3,
      safetyCheck: true
    },
    tasks: [
      {
        id: 'refactor-1',
        description: 'Converter CommonJS para ES Modules',
        action: 'convertModules',
        files: ['**/*.js']
      },
      {
        id: 'refactor-2',
        description: 'Adicionar TypeScript types',
        action: 'addTypes',
        files: ['**/*.js']
      }
    ]
  });
  
  console.log(`Refatoração concluída: ${result.successful} sucesso, ${result.failed} falhas`);
}
```

## 🧪 Testes

### Executar Testes
```bash
# Testes unitários
npm test

# Testes com cobertura
npm run test:coverage

# Testes de integração
npm run test:integration

# Testes E2E
npm run test:e2e

# Testes específicos do Modo Hive
npm run test:hive
```

### Estrutura de Testes
```javascript
// tests/unit/orchestrator.test.js
describe('AgentOrchestrator', () => {
  let orchestrator;
  
  beforeEach(() => {
    orchestrator = new AgentOrchestrator({
      maxConcurrentTasks: 2,
      enableHiveMode: true
    });
  });
  
  /**
   * TESTE: assignTask com agente válido
   * CENÁRIO: Atribuição bem-sucedida de tarefa
   * EXPECTATIVA: Tarefa deve ser adicionada à fila ativa
   */
  test('should assign task to available agent', async () => {
    const mockTask = {
      id: 'test-task-1',
      title: 'Test Task',
      priority: 'medium'
    };
    
    const result = await orchestrator.assignTask(mockTask, 'dev-backend');
    
    expect(result.status).toBe('assigned');
    expect(orchestrator.activeTasks.has('test-task-1')).toBe(true);
  });
  
  /**
   * TESTE: assignTask com agente inexistente
   * CENÁRIO: Tentativa de atribuição a agente não registrado
   * EXPECTATIVA: Deve lançar AgentNotFoundError
   */
  test('should throw error for non-existent agent', async () => {
    await expect(
      orchestrator.assignTask({ id: 'task-1' }, 'non-existent-agent')
    ).rejects.toThrow(AgentNotFoundError);
  });
});
```

// src/utils/logger.js
const winston = require('winston');

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp({
      format: 'YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss.SSS'
    }),
    winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  defaultMeta: {
    service: 'diyapp-core',
    version: 'v11.0.0'
  },
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: 'logs/error.log', 
      level: 'error',
      maxsize: 5242880, // 5MB
      maxFiles: 5
    }),
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: 'logs/combined.log',
      maxsize: 5242880,
      maxFiles: 10
    }),
    new winston.transports.Console({
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.colorize(),
        winston.format.simple()
      )
    })
  ]
});

// Uso padronizado
logger.info('Task started', {
  taskId: 'task_123',
  agent: 'dev-backend',
  action: 'code-generation',
  timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
});

logger.error('Hive mode conflict detected', {
  conflict: 'file-modification',
  files: ['src/agents/dev-backend/index.js'],
  resolution: 'rollback-applied',
  duration: '1500ms'
});
```

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Otimização de Performance

Vou configurar um sistema completo de otimização de performance com análise estática, otimização de bundles, caching estratégico e monitoramento de métricas.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```

│   │   ├── middleware/
│   │   ├── routes/
│   │   └── services/
│   └── shared/

### `.eslintrc.performance.js` (Configuração específica para performance)
```javascript
module.exports = {
  extends: './.eslintrc.js',
  rules: {
    // Regras específicas para otimização de performance
    'no-restricted-syntax': [
      'error',
      {
        selector: 'ForInStatement',
        message: 'for..in loops iterate over the entire prototype chain, which is slow. Use Object.{keys,values,entries} and iterate over the resulting array.'
      },
      {
        selector: 'ForOfStatement',
        message: 'for..of is slower than for loops. Use for loops for performance-critical code.'
      },
      {
        selector: 'Literal[value=null]',
        message: 'Use undefined instead of null for better performance.'
      }
    ],
    'max-depth': ['error', 4],
    'max-statements-per-line': ['error', { max: 2 }],
    'complexity': ['error', { max: 10 }],
    'max-params': ['error', 3],
    'no-nested-ternary': 'error',
    'no-unneeded-ternary': 'error',
    'prefer-destructuring': ['error', {
      array: false, // Arrays são mais rápidos sem destructuring
      object: true
    }]
  }
};
```
