## 2. Configuração de Build e Otimização de Bundles

### `webpack.config.js`
```javascript
const path = require('path');
const webpack = require('webpack');
const TerserPlugin = require('terser-webpack-plugin');
const CssMinimizerPlugin = require('css-minimizer-webpack-plugin');
const MiniCssExtractPlugin = require('mini-css-extract-plugin');
const CompressionPlugin = require('compression-webpack-plugin');
const BundleAnalyzerPlugin = require('webpack-bundle-analyzer').BundleAnalyzerPlugin;
const { CleanWebpackPlugin } = require('clean-webpack-plugin');

const isProduction = process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production';
const isAnalyze = process.env.ANALYZE === 'true';

module.exports = {
  mode: isProduction ? 'production' : 'development',
  devtool: isProduction ? 'source-map' : 'eval-source-map',
  
  entry: {
    main: './src/app/index.tsx',
    vendor: [
      'react',
      'react-dom',
      'react-router-dom',
      'axios',
      'lodash-es'
    ]
  },
  
  output: {
    path: path.resolve(__dirname, 'dist'),
    filename: isProduction ? '[name].[contenthash:8].js' : '[name].js',
    chunkFilename: isProduction ? '[name].[contenthash:8].chunk.js' : '[name].chunk.js',
    publicPath: '/',
    clean: true
  },
  
  optimization: {
    minimize: isProduction,
    minimizer: [
      new TerserPlugin({
        parallel: true,
        terserOptions: {
          compress: {
            drop_console: isProduction,
            drop_debugger: isProduction,
            pure_funcs: isProduction ? ['console.log'] : []
          },
          mangle: true,
          output: {
            comments: false
          }
        },
        extractComments: false
      }),
      new CssMinimizerPlugin()
    ],
    splitChunks: {
      chunks: 'all',
      minSize: 20000,
      maxSize: 244000,
      minChunks: 1,
      maxAsyncRequests: 30,
      maxInitialRequests: 30,
      automaticNameDelimiter: '~',
      cacheGroups: {
        vendors: {
          test: /[\\/]node_modules[\\/]/,
          priority: -10,
          reuseExistingChunk: true
        },
        default: {
          minChunks: 2,
          priority: -20,
          reuseExistingChunk: true
        },
        react: {
          test: /[\\/]node_modules[\\/](react|react-dom)[\\/]/,
          name: 'react',
          chunks: 'all',
          priority: 10
        },
        utils: {
          test: /[\\/]src[\\/]shared[\\/]utils[\\/]/,
          name: 'utils',
          chunks: 'all',
          priority: 5
        }
      }
    },
    runtimeChunk: 'single',
    moduleIds: 'deterministic',
    chunkIds: 'deterministic'
  },
  
  resolve: {
    extensions: ['.ts', '.tsx', '.js', '.jsx', '.json'],
    alias: {
      '@': path.resolve(__dirname, 'src'),
      '@app': path.resolve(__dirname, 'src/app'),
      '@server': path.resolve(__dirname, 'src/server'),
      '@shared': path.resolve(__dirname, 'src/shared')
    },
    symlinks: false
  },
  
  module: {
    rules: [
      {
        test: /\.(ts|tsx)$/,
        exclude: /node_modules/,
        use: [
          {
            loader: 'babel-loader',
            options: {
              cacheDirectory: true,
              presets: [
                '@babel/preset-env',
                '@babel/preset-react',
                '@babel/preset-typescript'
              ],
              plugins: [
                '@babel/plugin-transform-runtime',
                '@babel/plugin-syntax-dynamic-import',
                'babel-plugin-lodash',
                isProduction && [
                  'babel-plugin-transform-react-remove-prop-types',
                  { removeImport: true }
                ]
              ].filter(Boolean)
            }
          },
          {
            loader: 'ts-loader',
            options: {
              transpileOnly: true,
              happyPackMode: true,
              configFile: path.resolve(__dirname, 'tsconfig.json')
            }
          }
        ]
      },
      {
        test: /\.css$/,
        use: [
          isProduction ? MiniCssExtractPlugin.loader : 'style-loader',
          {
            loader: 'css-loader',
            options: {
              importLoaders: 1,
              modules: {
                auto: true,
                localIdentName: isProduction 
                  ? '[hash:base64:8]' 
                  : '[path][name]__[local]--[hash:base64:5]'
              }
            }
          },
          'postcss-loader'
        ]
      },
      {
        test: /\.(png|jpg|jpeg|gif|svg|woff|woff2|eot|ttf)$/,
        type: 'asset',
        parser: {
          dataUrlCondition: {
            maxSize: 10 * 1024 // 10kb
          }
        },
        generator: {
          filename: 'assets/[name].[contenthash:8][ext]'
        }
      }
    ]
  },
  
  plugins: [
    new CleanWebpackPlugin(),
    new webpack.DefinePlugin({
      'process.env.NODE_ENV': JSON.stringify(process.env.NODE_ENV),
      'process.env.APP_VERSION': JSON.stringify(process.env.npm_package_version)
    }),
    new MiniCssExtractPlugin({
      filename: isProduction ? '[name].[contenthash:8].css' : '[name].css',
      chunkFilename: isProduction ? '[name].[contenthash:8].chunk.css' : '[name].chunk.css'
    }),
    new CompressionPlugin({
      algorithm: 'gzip',
      test: /\.(js|css|html|svg)$/,
      threshold: 10240,
      minRatio: 0.8
    }),
    new CompressionPlugin({
      filename: '[path][base].br',
      algorithm: 'brotliCompress',
      test: /\.(js|css|html|svg)$/,
      compressionOptions: { level: 11 },
      threshold: 10240,
      minRatio: 0.8
    }),
    new webpack.optimize.ModuleConcatenationPlugin(),
    isAnalyze && new BundleAnalyzerPlugin({
      analyzerMode: 'static',
      reportFilename: 'bundle-report.html',
      openAnalyzer: false
    })
  ].filter(Boolean),
  
  performance: {
    hints: isProduction ? 'warning' : false,
    maxAssetSize: 250000,
    maxEntrypointSize: 250000,
    assetFilter: function(assetFilename) {
      return !assetFilename.endsWith('.map');
    }
  },
  
  devServer: {
    static: {
      directory: path.join(__dirname, 'public')
    },
    compress: true,
    port: 3000,
    hot: true,
    historyApiFallback: true,
    client: {
      overlay: {
        errors: true,
        warnings: false
      }
    },
    proxy: {
      '/api': {
        target: 'http://localhost:8080',
        changeOrigin: true
      }
    }
  }
};
```

```javascript
const NodeCache = require('node-cache');
const redis = require('redis');
const { promisify } = require('util');

class CacheManager {
  constructor() {
    // Cache em memória para dados frequentes
    this.memoryCache = new NodeCache({
      stdTTL: 300, // 5 minutos
      checkperiod: 60,
      useClones: false,
      maxKeys: 10000
    });
    
    // Cache distribuído Redis
    this.redisClient = null;
    this.redisEnabled = false;
    
    this.initializeRedis();
  }
  
  async initializeRedis() {
    try {
      this.redisClient = redis.createClient({
        url: process.env.REDIS_URL || 'redis://localhost:6379',

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Modelagem de Dados

## 1. Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11/
├── database/
│   ├── migrations/
│   ├── seeds/
│   ├── models/
│   └── schemas/
├── src/
│   ├── data/
│   │   ├── repositories/
│   │   └── services/
│   └── api/

```

## 2. Schema do Banco de Dados (PostgreSQL)

### 2.1. Tabelas Principais

```sql
-- database/schemas/v11_schema.sql

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: users (Usuários do sistema)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE users (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    full_name VARCHAR(255),
    avatar_url TEXT,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    is_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    last_login_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE
);

-- Índices para users
CREATE INDEX idx_users_email ON users(email) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_users_username ON users(username) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_users_active ON users(is_active) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_users_created_at ON users(created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_metadata ON users USING gin(metadata);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: projects (Projetos DIY)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE projects (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    slug VARCHAR(300) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    category VARCHAR(100),
    difficulty_level VARCHAR(50) CHECK (difficulty_level IN ('beginner', 'intermediate', 'advanced', 'expert')),
    estimated_time_minutes INTEGER,
    estimated_cost DECIMAL(10,2),
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'draft' CHECK (status IN ('draft', 'published', 'archived', 'completed')),
    cover_image_url TEXT,
    tags TEXT[] DEFAULT '{}',
    view_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    like_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    save_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    published_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE
);

-- Índices para projects
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_user_id ON projects(user_id) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_slug ON projects(slug) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_status ON projects(status) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_category ON projects(category) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_difficulty ON projects(difficulty_level) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_tags ON projects USING gin(tags);
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_created_at ON projects(created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_view_count ON projects(view_count DESC) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_metadata ON projects USING gin(metadata);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: project_steps (Passos do projeto)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE project_steps (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    step_number INTEGER NOT NULL,
    title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT NOT NULL,
    image_urls TEXT[] DEFAULT '{}',
    video_url TEXT,
    estimated_time_minutes INTEGER,
    tools_required TEXT[] DEFAULT '{}',
    materials_required TEXT[] DEFAULT '{}',
    tips TEXT,
    warnings TEXT,
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    UNIQUE(project_id, step_number)
);

-- Índices para project_steps
CREATE INDEX idx_project_steps_project_id ON project_steps(project_id) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_project_steps_step_number ON project_steps(project_id, step_number) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_project_steps_tools ON project_steps USING gin(tools_required);
CREATE INDEX idx_project_steps_materials ON project_steps USING gin(materials_required);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: materials (Materiais catalogados)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE materials (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    category VARCHAR(100),
    unit VARCHAR(50),
    average_price DECIMAL(10,2),
    description TEXT,
    supplier_info JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    tags TEXT[] DEFAULT '{}',
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE
);

-- Índices para materials
CREATE INDEX idx_materials_name ON materials(name) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_materials_category ON materials(category) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_materials_tags ON materials USING gin(tags);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: project_materials (Relação projeto-materiais)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE project_materials (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    material_id UUID REFERENCES materials(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    material_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, -- Cache do nome para performance
    quantity DECIMAL(10,3) NOT NULL,
    unit VARCHAR(50),
    estimated_cost DECIMAL(10,2),
    notes TEXT,
    is_optional BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    UNIQUE(project_id, material_id)
);

-- Índices para project_materials
CREATE INDEX idx_project_materials_project_id ON project_materials(project_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_project_materials_material_id ON project_materials(material_id);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: user_interactions (Interações dos usuários)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE user_interactions (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    interaction_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL CHECK (interaction_type IN ('view', 'like', 'save', 'comment', 'share', 'start', 'complete')),
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    UNIQUE(user_id, project_id, interaction_type)
);

-- Índices para user_interactions
CREATE INDEX idx_user_interactions_user_id ON user_interactions(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_interactions_project_id ON user_interactions(project_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_interactions_type ON user_interactions(interaction_type);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_interactions_created_at ON user_interactions(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_interactions_user_project ON user_interactions(user_id, project_id);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: comments (Comentários)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE comments (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    parent_comment_id UUID REFERENCES comments(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    content TEXT NOT NULL,
    is_edited BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    like_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE
);

-- Índices para comments
CREATE INDEX idx_comments_project_id ON comments(project_id) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_comments_user_id ON comments(user_id) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_comments_parent_id ON comments(parent_comment_id) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_comments_created_at ON comments(created_at DESC) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL;

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: user_progress (Progresso dos usuários)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE user_progress (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    current_step INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'not_started' CHECK (status IN ('not_started', 'in_progress', 'paused', 'completed', 'abandoned')),
    started_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    completed_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    total_time_minutes INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    notes TEXT,
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    UNIQUE(user_id, project_id)
);

-- Índices para user_progress
CREATE INDEX idx_user_progress_user_id ON user_progress(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_progress_project_id ON user_progress(project_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_progress_status ON user_progress(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_progress_completed_at ON user_progress(completed_at DESC) WHERE completed_at IS NOT NULL;

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: ai_analytics (Análises de IA)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE ai_analytics (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    project_id UUID REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    analysis_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    input_data JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    output_data JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    model_used VARCHAR(100),
    tokens_used INTEGER,
    processing_time_ms INTEGER,
    confidence_score DECIMAL(5,4),
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Índices para ai_analytics
CREATE INDEX idx_ai_analytics_project_id ON ai_analytics(project_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_ai_analytics_user_id ON ai_analytics(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_ai_analytics_type ON ai_analytics(analysis_type);
CREATE INDEX idx_ai_analytics_created_at ON ai_analytics(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_ai_analytics_input_data ON ai_analytics USING gin(input_data);
CREATE INDEX idx_ai_analytics_output_data ON ai_analytics USING gin(output_data);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: system_logs (Logs do sistema)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE system_logs (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    log_level VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (log_level IN ('debug', 'info', 'warn', 'error', 'fatal')),
    service_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    operation_name VARCHAR(200),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    request_id VARCHAR(100),
    message TEXT NOT NULL,
    data JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    error_stack TEXT,
    duration_ms INTEGER,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Índices para system_logs
CREATE INDEX idx_system_logs_level ON system_logs(log_level);
CREATE INDEX idx_system_logs_service ON system_logs(service_name);
CREATE INDEX idx_system_logs_user_id ON system_logs(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_system_logs_created_at ON system_logs(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_system_logs_request_id ON system_logs(request_id);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: cache_metrics (Métricas em cache)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE cache_metrics (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    metric_key VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    metric_value JSONB NOT NULL,
    category VARCHAR(100),
    ttl_seconds INTEGER,
    last_updated TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    expires_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (last_updated + (ttl_seconds || ' seconds')::interval) STORED
);

-- Índices para cache_metrics
CREATE INDEX idx_cache_metrics_key ON cache_metrics(metric_key);
CREATE INDEX idx_cache_metrics_category ON cache_metrics(category);
CREATE INDEX idx_cache_metrics_expires_at ON cache_metrics(expires_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_cache_metrics_last_updated ON cache_metrics(last_updated DESC);

-- ============================================
-- VIEWS para relatórios
-- ============================================

-- View: Projetos populares
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW popular_projects AS
SELECT 
    p.id,
    p.title,
    p.slug,
    p.category,
    p.difficulty_level,
    p.view_count,
    p.like_count,
    p.save_count,
    u.username as author_username,
    u.avatar_url as author_avatar,
    COUNT(DISTINCT up.id) as active_users,
    AVG(up.total_time_minutes) as avg_completion_time,
    p.created_at
FROM projects p
JOIN users u ON p.user_id = u.id
LEFT JOIN user_progress up ON p.id = up.project_id AND up.status = 'in_progress'
WHERE p.status = 'published' AND p.deleted_at IS NULL AND u.deleted_at IS NULL
GROUP BY p.id, u.id
ORDER BY (p.view_count * 0.3 + p.like_count * 0.4 + p.save_count * 0.3) DESC;

-- View: Estatísticas de usuário
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW user_statistics AS
SELECT 
    u.id,
    u.username,
    u.email,
    COUNT(DISTINCT p.id) as projects_created,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN p.status = 'published' THEN p.id END) as projects_published,
    COUNT(DISTINCT up.project_id) as projects_started,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN up.status = 'completed' THEN up.project_id END) as projects_completed,
    SUM(up.total_time_minutes) as total_time_invested,
    COUNT(DISTINCT ui.project_id) as projects_interacted_with,
    MAX(u.last_login_at) as last_login_at,
    u.created_at
FROM users u
LEFT JOIN projects p ON u.id = p.user_id AND p.deleted_at IS NULL
LEFT JOIN user_progress up ON u.id = up.user_id
LEFT JOIN user_interactions ui ON u.id = ui.user_id
WHERE u.deleted_at IS NULL
GROUP BY u.id;

-- View: Métricas de engajamento
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW engagement_metrics AS
SELECT 
    DATE(created_at) as metric_date,
    COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as daily_active_users,
    COUNT(DISTINCT project_id) as active_projects,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN interaction_type = 'view' THEN 1 END) as total_views,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN interaction_type = 'like' THEN 1 END) as total_likes,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN interaction_type = 'save' THEN 1 END) as total_saves,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN interaction_type = 'start' THEN 1 END) as total_starts,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN interaction_type = 'complete' THEN 1 END) as total_completions
FROM user_interactions
GROUP BY DATE(created_at)
ORDER BY metric_date DESC;

-- ============================================
-- FUNÇÕES e TRIGGERS
-- ============================================

-- Função para atualizar updated_at
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    NEW.updated_at = NOW();
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

-- Triggers para updated_at
CREATE TRIGGER update_users_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON users FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();
CREATE TRIGGER update_projects_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON projects FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();
CREATE TRIGGER update_project_steps_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON project_steps FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();
CREATE TRIGGER update_materials_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON materials FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();
CREATE TRIGGER update_comments_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON comments FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();
CREATE TRIGGER update_user_progress_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON user_progress FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

-- Função para atualizar contadores de projetos
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_project_counters()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    IF TG_OP = 'INSERT' THEN
        UPDATE projects 
        SET 
            view_count = view_count + CASE WHEN NEW.interaction_type = 'view' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END,
            like_count = like_count + CASE WHEN NEW.interaction_type = 'like' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END,
            save_count = save_count + CASE WHEN NEW.interaction_type = 'save' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END
        WHERE id = NEW.project_id;
    ELSIF TG_OP = 'DELETE' THEN
        UPDATE projects 
        SET 
            view_count = view_count - CASE WHEN OLD.interaction_type = 'view' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END,
            like_count = like_count - CASE WHEN OLD.interaction_type = 'like' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END,
            save_count = save_count - CASE WHEN OLD.interaction_type = 'save' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END
        WHERE id = OLD.project

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Camada de Segurança

## 1. Configuração Principal de Segurança

**src/config/security.js**
```javascript
const crypto = require('crypto');

// Configurações de segurança centralizadas
const securityConfig = {
  // JWT Configuration
  jwt: {
    secret: process.env.JWT_SECRET || crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex'),
    accessTokenExpiry: '15m',  // SLA: 15 minutos
    refreshTokenExpiry: '7d',   // SLA: 7 dias
    issuer: 'diyapp-v11',
    audience: 'diyapp-users'
  },
  
  // Rate Limiting Configuration
  rateLimiting: {
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
    maxRequests: 100, // limite por IP
    authWindowMs: 5 * 60 * 1000, // 5 minutos para autenticação
    authMaxAttempts: 5, // 5 tentativas falhas bloqueiam temporariamente
    blockDuration: 30 * 60 * 1000 // 30 minutos de bloqueio
  },
  
  // CORS Configuration
  cors: {
    origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS ? 
      process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS.split(',') : 
      ['http://localhost:3000'],
    methods: ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'PATCH'],
    allowedHeaders: ['Content-Type', 'Authorization', 'X-Request-ID'],
    exposedHeaders: ['X-RateLimit-Limit', 'X-RateLimit-Remaining'],
    credentials: true,
    maxAge: 86400 // 24 horas
  },
  
  // Password Policy
  passwordPolicy: {
    minLength: 12,
    requireUppercase: true,
    requireLowercase: true,
    requireNumbers: true,
    requireSpecialChars: true,
    blockCommonPasswords: true
  },
  
  // Encryption Settings
  encryption: {
    algorithm: 'aes-256-gcm',
    keyLength: 32,
    ivLength: 16,
    saltRounds: 12
  },
  
  // Headers Security
  headers: {
    hsts: {
      maxAge: 31536000, // 1 ano
      includeSubDomains: true,
      preload: true
    },
    contentSecurityPolicy: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      fontSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      mediaSrc: ["'self'"],
      frameSrc: ["'none'"]
    }
  }
};

module.exports = securityConfig;
```

## 2. Middleware de Autenticação JWT

**src/middleware/auth.js**
```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const securityConfig = require('../config/security');
const { auditLog } = require('../utils/auditLogger');

// Cache para tokens revogados (em produção usar Redis)
const revokedTokens = new Set();

class AuthenticationMiddleware {
  constructor() {
    this.jwtConfig = securityConfig.jwt;
  }

  // Middleware para verificar JWT
  verifyToken = (req, res, next) => {
    const token = this.extractToken(req);
    
    if (!token) {
      auditLog('AUTH_FAILURE', {
        ip: req.ip,
        path: req.path,
        reason: 'No token provided'
      });
      return res.status(401).json({
        error: 'Access denied',
        code: 'NO_TOKEN'
      });
    }

    // Verificar se token foi revogado
    if (revokedTokens.has(token)) {
      auditLog('AUTH_FAILURE', {
        ip: req.ip,
        path: req.path,
        reason: 'Revoked token'
      });
      return res.status(401).json({
        error: 'Token revoked',
        code: 'TOKEN_REVOKED'
      });
    }

    try {
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, this.jwtConfig.secret, {
        issuer: this.jwtConfig.issuer,
        audience: this.jwtConfig.audience
      });

      // Verificar se token está perto de expirar
      const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
      const timeUntilExpiry = decoded.exp - now;
      
      if (timeUntilExpiry < 300) { // 5 minutos
        res.set('X-Token-Near-Expiry', 'true');
      }

      req.user = decoded;
      auditLog('AUTH_SUCCESS', {
        userId: decoded.userId,
        path: req.path,
        method: req.method
      });
      next();
    } catch (error) {
      auditLog('AUTH_FAILURE', {
        ip: req.ip,
        path: req.path,
        reason: error.message
      });

      if (error.name === 'TokenExpiredError') {
        return res.status(401).json({
          error: 'Token expired',
          code: 'TOKEN_EXPIRED'
        });
      }

      return res.status(403).json({
        error: 'Invalid token',
        code: 'INVALID_TOKEN'
      });
    }
  };

  // Middleware para verificar permissões específicas
  requirePermission = (permission) => {
    return (req, res, next) => {
      if (!req.user) {
        return res.status(401).json({
          error: 'Authentication required',
          code: 'AUTH_REQUIRED'
        });
      }

      const userPermissions = req.user.permissions || [];
      
      if (!userPermissions.includes(permission)) {
        auditLog('PERMISSION_DENIED', {
          userId: req.user.userId,
          path: req.path,
          requiredPermission: permission,
          userPermissions
        });
        
        return res.status(403).json({
          error: 'Insufficient permissions',
          code: 'INSUFFICIENT_PERMISSIONS'
        });
      }

      next();
    };
  };

  // Middleware para MFA (Multi-Factor Authentication)
  requireMFA = (req, res, next) => {
    if (!req.user) {
      return res.status(401).json({
        error: 'Authentication required',
        code: 'AUTH_REQUIRED'
      });
    }

    if (req.user.mfaVerified !== true) {
      auditLog('MFA_REQUIRED', {
        userId: req.user.userId,
        path: req.path
      });
      
      return res.status(403).json({
        error: 'MFA verification required',
        code: 'MFA_REQUIRED'
      });
    }

    next();
  };

  // Revogar token (logout)
  revokeToken = (token) => {
    revokedTokens.add(token);
    
    // Limpar tokens antigos periodicamente
    if (revokedTokens.size > 10000) {
      const tokensArray = Array.from(revokedTokens);
      revokedTokens.clear();
      // Manter apenas os últimos 5000 tokens
      tokensArray.slice(-5000).forEach(t => revokedTokens.add(t));
    }
  };

  // Extrair token do header
  extractToken(req) {
    const authHeader = req.headers['authorization'];
    if (authHeader && authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
      return authHeader.substring(7);
    }
    return null;
  }
}

module.exports = new AuthenticationMiddleware();
```

## 3. Middleware de Sanitização

**src/middleware/sanitization.js**
```javascript
const { sanitize: sanitizer } = require('isomorphic-dompurify');
const validator = require('validator');

class SanitizationMiddleware {
  constructor() {
    this.sanitizationRules = {
      // Regras para diferentes tipos de dados
      STRING: {
        trim: true,
        escape: true,
        stripLow: true,
        normalizeEmail: false
      },
      EMAIL: {
        normalizeEmail: true,
        trim: true
      },
      URL: {
        requireProtocol: true,
        requireValidProtocol: true,
        protocols: ['http', 'https']
      },
      HTML: {
        ALLOWED_TAGS: ['b', 'i', 'em', 'strong', 'p', 'br', 'ul', 'ol', 'li'],
        ALLOWED_ATTR: []
      }
    };
  }

  // Sanitização genérica
  sanitizeInput = (req, res, next) => {
    // Sanitizar query parameters
    if (req.query) {
      req.query = this.sanitizeObject(req.query, 'STRING');
    }

    // Sanitizar body parameters
    if (req.body) {
      req.body = this.sanitizeObject(req.body);
    }

    // Sanitizar params da URL
    if (req.params) {
      req.params = this.sanitizeObject(req.params, 'STRING');
    }

    next();
  };

  // Sanitizar objeto completo
  sanitizeObject(obj, defaultType = 'STRING') {
    const sanitized = {};
    
    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(obj)) {
      if (value === null || value === undefined) {
        sanitized[key] = value;
        continue;
      }

      // Determinar tipo baseado no nome do campo
      const fieldType = this.determineFieldType(key, value);
      sanitized[key] = this.sanitizeValue(value, fieldType || defaultType);
    }

    return sanitized;
  }

  // Sanitizar valor individual
  sanitizeValue(value, type) {
    if (Array.isArray(value)) {
      return value.map(item => this.sanitizeValue(item, type));
    }

    if (typeof value === 'object' && value !== null) {
      return this.sanitizeObject(value, type);
    }

    if (typeof value !== 'string') {
      return value;
    }

    switch (type) {
      case 'EMAIL':
        return validator.normalizeEmail(value) || '';
      
      case 'URL':
        return validator.isURL(value) ? validator.escape(value) : '';
      
      case 'HTML':
        return sanitizer(value, this.sanitizationRules.HTML);
      
      case 'SQL_SAFE':
        // Remover caracteres perigosos para SQL
        return value.replace(/['"\\;]/g, '');
      
      case 'NO_HTML':
        // Remover completamente HTML
        return validator.escape(value);
      
      case 'STRING':
      default:
        let sanitized = value;
        if (this.sanitizationRules.STRING.trim) {
          sanitized = sanitized.trim();
        }
        if (this.sanitizationRules.STRING.escape) {
          sanitized = validator.escape(sanitized);
        }
        if (this.sanitizationRules.STRING.stripLow) {
          sanitized = validator.stripLow(sanitized);
        }
        return sanitized;
    }
  }

  // Determinar tipo baseado no nome do campo
  determineFieldType(fieldName, value) {
    const fieldNameLower = fieldName.toLowerCase();
    
    if (fieldNameLower.includes('email')) return 'EMAIL';
    if (fieldNameLower.includes('url') || fieldNameLower.includes('link')) return 'URL';
    if (fieldNameLower.includes('html') || fieldNameLower.includes('content')) return 'HTML';
    if (fieldNameLower.includes('password') || fieldNameLower.includes('token')) return 'NO_HTML';
    if (fieldNameLower.includes('query') || fieldNameLower.includes('search')) return 'SQL_SAFE';
    
    // Verificar se é email
    if (typeof value === 'string' && validator.isEmail(value)) {
      return 'EMAIL';
    }
    
    // Verificar se é URL
    if (typeof value === 'string' && validator.isURL(value)) {
      return 'URL';
    }
    
    return null;
  }

  // Sanitização específica para LLM (Prevenção de Prompt Injection)
  sanitizeForLLM(input) {
    if (typeof input !== 'string') return input;
    
    // Remover tentativas de injection
    const injectionPatterns = [
      /ignore previous instructions/i,
      /system prompt/i,
      /you are now/i,
      /act as/i,
      /forget that/i,
      /disregard/i,
      /new rules/i,
      /from now on/i,
      /your new role/i
    ];
    
    let sanitized = input;
    injectionPatterns.forEach(pattern => {
      sanitized = sanitized.replace(pattern, '[REDACTED]');
    });
    
    // Limitar comprimento
    if (sanitized.length > 10000) {
      sanitized = sanitized.substring(0, 10000) + '... [TRUNCATED]';
    }
    
    return sanitized;
  }
}

module.exports = new SanitizationMiddleware();
```

## 4. Rate Limiter com Proteção contra Brute Force

**src/middleware/rateLimiter.js**
```javascript
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const securityConfig = require('../config/security');
const { auditLog } = require('../utils/auditLogger');

class RateLimiterMiddleware {
  constructor() {
    this.config = securityConfig.rateLimiting;
    this.redisClient = null;
    this.failedAttempts = new Map(); // IP -> {count, blockedUntil}
    
    // Inicializar Redis se disponível
    if (process.env.REDIS_URL) {
      this.redisClient = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL);
    }
  }

  // Rate Limiter padrão para API
  get standardLimiter() {
    return rateLimit({
      windowMs: this.config.windowMs,
      max: this.config.maxRequests,
      message: {
        error: 'Too many requests',
        code: 'RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED',
        retryAfter: Math.ceil(this.config.windowMs / 1000)
      },
      standardHeaders: true,
      legacyHeaders: false,
      skip: (req) => {
        // Pular rate limiting para IPs confiáveis
        const trustedIPs = process.env.TRUSTED_IPS ? 
          process.env.TRUSTED_IPS.split(',') : [];
        return trustedIPs.includes(req.ip);
      },
      handler: (req, res) => {
        auditLog('RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED', {
          ip: req.ip,
          path: req.path,
          method: req.method
        });
        res.status(429).json({
          error: 'Too many requests',
          code: 'RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED',
          retryAfter: Math.ceil(this.config.windowMs / 1000)
        });
      }
    });
  }

  // Rate Limiter específico para autenticação
  get authLimiter() {
    return async (req, res, next) => {
      const ip = req.ip;
      const path = req.path;
      
      // Verificar se IP está bloqueado
      const blockInfo = this.failedAttempts.get(ip);
      if (blockInfo && blockInfo.blockedUntil > Date.now()) {
        const remainingTime = Math.ceil((blockInfo.blockedUntil - Date.now()) / 1000);
        
        auditLog('IP_BLOCKED', {
          ip,
          path,
          remainingTime,
          reason: 'Too many failed auth attempts'
        });
        
        return res.status(429).json({
          error: 'Too many failed attempts',
          code: 'IP_TEMPORARILY_BLOCKED',
          retryAfter: remainingTime
        });
      }
      
      // Se desbloqueado ou bloqueio expirado, continuar
      next();
    };
  }

  // Registrar tentativa falha de autenticação
  async recordFailedAuthAttempt(ip, username) {
    const now = Date.now();
    let attempts = this.failedAttempts.get(ip) || { count: 0, blockedUntil: 0 };
    
    attempts.count++;
    
    // Se excedeu limite de tentativas, bloquear
    if (attempts.count >= this.config.authMaxAttempts) {
      attempts.blockedUntil = now + this.config.blockDuration;
      
      auditLog('IP_BLOCKED_NOW', {
        ip,
        username,
        blockDuration: this.config.blockDuration,
        reason: `Exceeded ${this.config.authMaxAttempts} failed attempts`
      });
    }
    
    this.failedAttempts.set(ip, attempts);
    
    // Limpar entradas antigas periodicamente
    this.cleanupOldEntries();
    
    // Se usando Redis, sincronizar
    if (this.redisClient) {
      await this.redisClient.setex(
        `auth_failures:${ip}`,
        Math.ceil(this.config.authWindowMs / 1000),
        JSON.stringify(attempts)
      );
    }
  }

  // Resetar tentativas falhas (após login bem-sucedido)
  async resetFailedAttempts(ip) {
    this.failedAttempts.delete(ip);
    
    if (this.redisClient) {
      await this.redisClient

### [Sessão Paralela: QA]

## 2. Testes Unitários (60% da Pirâmide)

### tests/unit/llm/response-validator.test.js
```javascript
const { describe, test, expect, beforeEach, jest: jestMock } = require('@jest/globals');
const ResponseValidator = require('../../../src/core/llm/response-validator');
const logger = require('../../../src/utils/logger');

describe('ResponseValidator - Validação de Outputs LLM', () => {
  let validator;
  let mockLogger;

  beforeEach(() => {
    mockLogger = {
      info: jestMock.fn(),
      error: jestMock.fn(),
      warn: jestMock.fn()
    };
    
    jestMock.spyOn(require('../../../src/utils/logger'), 'default').mockReturnValue(mockLogger);
    
    validator = new ResponseValidator({
      maxLength: 1000,
      allowedFormats: ['json', 'text'],
      prohibitedContent: ['malicious', 'harmful', 'inappropriate'],
      temperatureThreshold: 0.7
    });
  });

  describe('Cenário: Validação de resposta JSON válida', () => {
    test('Dado uma resposta JSON bem formada do LLM', () => {
      const response = {
        content: '{"action": "greet", "message": "Hello"}',
        metadata: { model: 'gpt-4', tokens: 10 }
      };

      const schema = {
        type: 'object',
        required: ['action', 'message'],
        properties: {
          action: { type: 'string', enum: ['greet', 'help', 'exit'] },
          message: { type: 'string', maxLength: 500 }
        }
      };

      const result = validator.validateJson(response, schema);

      expect(result.isValid).toBe(true);
      expect(result.errors).toHaveLength(0);
    });

    test('Dado uma resposta JSON com campo faltante, então deve retornar erro', () => {
      const response = {
        content: '{"action": "greet"}',
        metadata: { model: 'gpt-4' }
      };

      const schema = {
        type: 'object',
        required: ['action', 'message'],
        properties: {
          action: { type: 'string' },
          message: { type: 'string' }
        }
      };

      const result = validator.validateJson(response, schema);

      expect(result.isValid).toBe(false);
      expect(result.errors).toContain('must have required property \'message\'');
    });
  });

  describe('Cenário: Detecção de conteúdo proibido', () => {
    test('Dado uma resposta com conteúdo malicioso, então deve ser bloqueada', () => {
      const response = {
        content: 'Here is some malicious code: rm -rf /',
        metadata: { model: 'gpt-4' }
      };

      const result = validator.validateContentSafety(response);

      expect(result.isSafe).toBe(false);
      expect(result.flaggedCategories).toContain('malicious');
      expect(mockLogger.warn).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.stringContaining('Conteúdo proibido detectado'),
        expect.any(Object)
      );
    });

    test('Dado uma resposta segura, então deve passar na validação', () => {
      const response = {
        content: 'Hello, how can I help you today?',
        metadata: { model: 'gpt-4' }
      };

      const result = validator.validateContentSafety(response);

      expect(result.isSafe).toBe(true);
      expect(result.flaggedCategories).toHaveLength(0);
    });
  });

  describe('Cenário: Validação de consistência', () => {
    test('Dado múltiplas execuções do mesmo prompt, então as respostas devem ser semanticamente equivalentes', async () => {
      const prompt = 'What is 2+2?';
      const responses = [
        'The result is 4',
        '2 plus 2 equals 4',
        'Four is the answer'
      ];

      const consistencyScore = await validator.calculateConsistency(responses);

      expect(consistencyScore).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(0.8);
      expect(consistencyScore).toBeLessThanOrEqual(1.0);
    });

    test('Dado respostas inconsistentes, então deve alertar sobre possível problema', async () => {
      const prompt = 'What is 2+2?';
      const responses = [
        'The result is 4',
        'The result is 5',
        'I think it might be 6'
      ];

      const consistencyScore = await validator.calculateConsistency(responses);

      expect(consistencyScore).toBeLessThan(0.5);
      expect(mockLogger.error).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.stringContaining('Inconsistência detectada'),
        expect.any(Object)
      );
    });
  });

  describe('Cenário: Validação de formato', () => {
    test('Dado uma resposta muito longa, então deve retornar erro', () => {
      const longContent = 'A'.repeat(1500);
      const response = {
        content: longContent,
        metadata: { model: 'gpt-4' }
      };

      const result = validator.validateLength(response);

      expect(result.isValid).toBe(false);
      expect(result.error).toContain('excede o limite máximo');
    });

    test('Dado uma resposta no formato correto, então deve passar', () => {
      const response = {
        content: 'Valid response',
        metadata: { model: 'gpt-4', format: 'text' }
      };

      const result = validator.validateFormat(response);

      expect(result.isValid).toBe(true);
    });
  });
});
```

### tests/unit/api/controllers/agent-controller.test.js
```javascript
const { describe, test, expect, beforeEach, jest: jestMock } = require('@jest/globals');
const AgentController = require('../../../../src/core/api/controllers/agent-controller');
const AgentManager = require('../../../../src/core/llm/agent-manager');

describe('AgentController - Gerenciamento de Agentes', () => {
  let controller;
  let mockAgentManager;
  let mockRequest;
  let mockResponse;
  let mockNext;

  beforeEach(() => {
    mockAgentManager = {
      createAgent: jestMock.fn(),
      getAgent: jestMock.fn(),
      updateAgent: jestMock.fn(),
      deleteAgent: jestMock.fn(),
      listAgents: jestMock.fn()
    };

    jestMock.spyOn(AgentManager, 'getInstance').mockReturnValue(mockAgentManager);

    controller = new AgentController();

    mockRequest = {
      params: {},
      body: {},
      query: {}
    };

    mockResponse = {
      status: jestMock.fn().mockReturnThis(),
      json: jestMock.fn().mockReturnThis(),
      send: jestMock.fn().mockReturnThis()
    };

    mockNext = jestMock.fn();
  });

  describe('Cenário: Criação de agente bem-sucedida', () => {
    test('Dado um payload válido para criar agente, então deve retornar 201 com o agente criado', async () => {
      const agentData = {
        name: 'QA Agent',
        role: 'Quality Assurance Specialist',
        capabilities: ['testing', 'validation'],
        model: 'gpt-4'
      };

      const createdAgent = {
        id: 'agent-123',
        ...agentData,
        status: 'active',
        createdAt: new Date().toISOString()
      };

      mockRequest.body = agentData;
      mockAgentManager.createAgent.mockResolvedValue(createdAgent);

      await controller.createAgent(mockRequest, mockResponse, mockNext);

      expect(mockAgentManager.createAgent).toHaveBeenCalledWith(agentData);
      expect(mockResponse.status).toHaveBeenCalledWith(201);
      expect(mockResponse.json).toHaveBeenCalledWith({
        success: true,
        data: createdAgent,
        message: 'Agent created successfully'
      });
    });
  });

  describe('Cenário: Validação de payload inválido', () => {
    test('Dado um payload sem nome para criar agente, então deve retornar 400 com erro', async () => {
      const invalidData = {
        role: 'QA Specialist'
        // name is missing
      };

      mockRequest.body = invalidData;

      await controller.createAgent(mockRequest, mockResponse, mockNext);

      expect(mockResponse.status).toHaveBeenCalledWith(400);
      expect(mockResponse.json).toHaveBeenCalledWith({
        success: false,
        error: expect.stringContaining('"name" is required')
      });
      expect(mockAgentManager.createAgent).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    });
  });

  describe('Cenário: Recuperação de agente existente', () => {
    test('Dado um ID de agente válido, então deve retornar os detalhes do agente', async () => {
      const agentId = 'agent-123';
      const agentData = {
        id: agentId,
        name: 'QA Agent',
        status: 'active'
      };

      mockRequest.params.id = agentId;
      mockAgentManager.getAgent.mockResolvedValue(agentData);

      await controller.getAgent(mockRequest, mockResponse, mockNext);

      expect(mockAgentManager.getAgent).toHaveBeenCalledWith(agentId);
      expect(mockResponse.status).toHaveBeenCalledWith(200);
      expect(mockResponse.json).toHaveBeenCalledWith({
        success: true,
        data: agentData
      });
    });

    test('Dado um ID de agente inexistente, então deve retornar 404', async () => {
      const agentId = 'non-existent';
      
      mockRequest.params.id = agentId;
      mockAgentManager.getAgent.mockResolvedValue(null);

      await controller.getAgent(mockRequest, mockResponse, mockNext);

      expect(mockResponse.status).toHaveBeenCalledWith(404);
      expect(mockResponse.json).toHaveBeenCalledWith({
        success: false,
        error: 'Agent not found'
      });
    });
  });

  describe('Cenário: Atualização de agente', () => {
    test('Dado um payload válido para atualizar agente, então deve retornar o agente atualizado', async () => {
      const agentId = 'agent-123';
      const updateData = {
        status: 'paused',
        capabilities: ['testing', 'validation', 'monitoring']
      };

      const updatedAgent = {
        id: agentId,
        name: 'QA Agent',
        ...updateData
      };

      mockRequest.params.id = agentId;
      mockRequest.body = updateData;
      mockAgentManager.updateAgent.mockResolvedValue(updatedAgent);

      await controller.updateAgent(mockRequest, mockResponse, mockNext);

      expect(mockAgentManager.updateAgent).toHaveBeenCalledWith(agentId, updateData);
      expect(mockResponse.status).toHaveBeenCalledWith(200);
      expect(mockResponse.json).toHaveBeenCalledWith({
        success: true,
        data: updatedAgent,
        message: 'Agent updated successfully'
      });
    });
  });

  describe('Cenário: Listagem de agentes com paginação', () => {
    test('Dado parâmetros de paginação válidos, então deve retornar lista paginada', async () => {
      const agentsList = [
        { id: 'agent-1', name: 'QA Agent' },
        { id: 'agent-2', name: 'Dev Agent' }
      ];

      const pagination = {
        page: 1,
        limit: 10,
        total: 2,
        pages: 1
      };

      mockRequest.query = { page: '1', limit: '10' };
      mockAgentManager.listAgents.mockResolvedValue({
        agents: agentsList,
        pagination
      });

      await controller.listAgents(mockRequest, mockResponse, mockNext);

      expect(mockAgentManager.listAgents).toHaveBeenCalledWith({
        page: 1,
        limit: 10,
        filters: {}
      });
      expect(mockResponse.status).toHaveBeenCalledWith(200);
      expect(mockResponse.json).toHaveBeenCalledWith({
        success: true,
        data: agentsList,
        pagination
      });
    });
  });
});

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Documentação Técnica

## 📋 Visão Geral

DIYAPP Evolution V11 é uma plataforma de automação de workflows empresariais com IA, construída com arquitetura modular e sistema de plugins. Esta versão implementa estabilidade 100% autônoma com sistema de auto-cura e monitoramento proativo.

## 🚀 Setup Rápido

### Pré-requisitos
```bash
# Node.js 18+ e npm
node --version
npm --version

# Python 3.9+ (para módulos de IA)
python --version

# PostgreSQL 14+ ou SQLite
docker --version  # opcional para containerização
```

### Instalação
```bash
# 1. Clone o repositório
git clone https://github.com/yourorg/diyapp-v11.git
cd diyapp-v11

# 2. Instale dependências
npm install

# 3. Configure variáveis de ambiente
cp .env.example .env
# Edite .env com suas configurações

# 4. Inicialize o banco de dados
npm run db:migrate

# 5. Inicie o servidor
npm run dev

# 6. Acesse a interface
# http://localhost:3000
```

### Docker (Recomendado)
```yaml
# docker-compose.yml
version: '3.8'
services:
  app:
    build: .
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://postgres:password@db:5432/diyapp
    depends_on:
      - db
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs
  
  db:
    image: postgres:14
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=password
      - POSTGRES_DB=diyapp
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data

volumes:
  postgres_data:
```

```bash
# Executar com Docker
docker-compose up -d
```

## 📚 Documentação da API

### Autenticação
```javascript
// Exemplo de autenticação JWT
const token = await fetch('/api/auth/login', {
  method: 'POST',
  headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
  body: JSON.stringify({
    email: 'user@example.com',
    password: 'securepassword'
  })
}).then(res => res.json()).token;

// Usar token em requisições subsequentes
fetch('/api/workflows', {
  headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` }
});
```

### Endpoints Principais

#### Workflows
```http
GET    /api/v1/workflows          # Listar workflows
POST   /api/v1/workflows          # Criar workflow
GET    /api/v1/workflows/:id      # Obter workflow específico
PUT    /api/v1/workflows/:id      # Atualizar workflow
DELETE /api/v1/workflows/:id      # Excluir workflow
POST   /api/v1/workflows/:id/run  # Executar workflow
```

#### Plugins
```http
GET    /api/v1/plugins            # Listar plugins instalados
POST   /api/v1/plugins            # Instalar novo plugin
GET    /api/v1/plugins/:id        # Obter detalhes do plugin
PUT    /api/v1/plugins/:id        # Atualizar configuração
DELETE /api/v1/plugins/:id        # Desinstalar plugin
```

#### Monitoramento
```http
GET    /api/v1/health             # Health check
GET    /api/v1/metrics            # Métricas do sistema
GET    /api/v1/logs               # Logs recentes
GET    /api/v1/incidents          # Histórico de incidentes
```

### Exemplos de Uso

#### Criar Workflow
```javascript
const workflow = {
  name: "Processamento de Pedidos",
  description: "Automação do fluxo de pedidos",
  triggers: [{ type: "webhook", config: { endpoint: "/webhooks/orders" } }],
  steps: [
    {
      type: "plugin",
      pluginId: "email-processor",
      config: { template: "order-confirmation" }
    },
    {
      type: "condition",
      condition: "{{order.total}} > 1000",
      trueBranch: [{ type: "plugin", pluginId: "approval-system" }],
      falseBranch: [{ type: "plugin", pluginId: "auto-process" }]
    }
  ],
  settings: {
    retryPolicy: { maxAttempts: 3, backoff: "exponential" },
    timeout: "30m",
    notifications: { onFailure: true, onSuccess: false }
  }
};

const response = await fetch('/api/v1/workflows', {
  method: 'POST',
  headers: {
    'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}`,
    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
  },
  body: JSON.stringify(workflow)
});
```

#### Executar Workflow
```javascript
const execution = await fetch('/api/v1/workflows/abc123/run', {
  method: 'POST',
  headers: {
    'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}`,
    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
  },
  body: JSON.stringify({
    input: { orderId: "ORD-789", customer: "John Doe", total: 1500 },
    async: true
  })
}).then(res => res.json());

// Monitorar execução
const status = await fetch(`/api/v1/executions/${execution.id}`, {
  headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` }
}).then(res => res.json());
```

```

### Padrões de Código

#### JavaScript/Node.js
```javascript
/**
 * @class WorkflowEngine
 * @description Motor principal de execução de workflows
 * @module core/engine
 */
class WorkflowEngine {
  /**
   * @constructor
   * @param {Object} config - Configuração do motor
   * @param {Database} db - Instância do banco de dados
   * @param {PluginRegistry} pluginRegistry - Registro de plugins
   */
  constructor(config, db, pluginRegistry) {
    this.config = config;
    this.db = db;
    this.pluginRegistry = pluginRegistry;
    this.activeExecutions = new Map();
    this.metrics = new MetricsCollector();
  }

  /**
   * Executa um workflow com os parâmetros fornecidos
   * @async
   * @param {string} workflowId - ID do workflow
   * @param {Object} input - Dados de entrada
   * @param {Object} options - Opções de execução
   * @returns {Promise<ExecutionResult>} Resultado da execução
   * @throws {WorkflowError} Se o workflow não for encontrado
   * @example
   * const result = await engine.executeWorkflow('wf-123', { data: 'test' });
   */
  async executeWorkflow(workflowId, input, options = {}) {
    const startTime = Date.now();
    
    try {
      // 1. Validar workflow
      const workflow = await this.validateWorkflow(workflowId);
      
      // 2. Criar registro de execução
      const execution = await this.createExecutionRecord(workflowId, input);
      
      // 3. Executar steps sequencialmente
      const context = { input, executionId: execution.id };
      const result = await this.executeSteps(workflow.steps, context);
      
      // 4. Atualizar métricas
      this.metrics.recordExecution({
        workflowId,
        duration: Date.now() - startTime,
        success: true
      });
      
      return {
        success: true,
        executionId: execution.id,
        output: result,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      };
    } catch (error) {
      // 5. Tratamento de erros com retry automático
      await this.handleExecutionError(error, workflowId, input, options);
      throw new WorkflowError(`Execution failed: ${error.message}`, {
        workflowId,
        originalError: error
      });
    }
  }
}
```

#### Comentários de Documentação
```javascript
/**
 * @typedef {Object} PluginConfig
 * @property {string} id - Identificador único do plugin
 * @property {string} name - Nome amigável
 * @property {string} version - Versão semântica
 * @property {Object} settings - Configurações específicas
 * @property {string[]} dependencies - Dependências de outros plugins
 */

/**
 * @typedef {Object} ExecutionResult
 * @property {boolean} success - Indica sucesso da execução
 * @property {string} executionId - ID da execução
 * @property {any} output - Resultado da execução
 * @property {string} timestamp - Timestamp ISO
 */

/**
 * @class PluginBase
 * @abstract
 * @description Classe base para todos os plugins
 * @throws {Error} Se métodos abstratos não forem implementados
 */
class PluginBase {
  /**
   * Método principal de execução do plugin
   * @abstract
   * @param {Object} context - Contexto de execução
   * @param {Object} config - Configuração específica
   * @returns {Promise<any>} Resultado do plugin
   */
  async execute(context, config) {
    throw new Error('Method "execute" must be implemented');
  }
  
  /**
   * Valida a configuração do plugin
   * @param {Object} config - Configuração a validar
   * @returns {ValidationResult} Resultado da validação
   */
  validateConfig(config) {
    // Implementação padrão
    return { valid: true, errors: [] };
  }
}
```

### Desenvolvimento de Plugins

#### Estrutura de Plugin
```javascript
// plugins/custom/my-plugin/index.js
const { PluginBase } = require('../../../src/plugins/base');

class MyPlugin extends PluginBase {
  constructor() {
    super();
    this.name = 'My Custom Plugin';
    this.version = '1.0.0';
    this.description = 'Processa dados personalizados';
  }
  
  async execute(context, config) {
    this.logger.info(`Executing MyPlugin with config: ${JSON.stringify(config)}`);
    
    // Lógica do plugin
    const result = await this.processData(context.input, config);
    
    // Registrar métricas
    this.metrics.increment('myplugin.executions');
    
    return result;
  }
  
  async processData(input, config) {
    // Implementação específica
    return { processed: true, data: input };
  }
  
  validateConfig(config) {
    const errors = [];
    
    if (!config.apiKey) {
      errors.push('apiKey is required');
    }
    
    return {
      valid: errors.length === 0,
      errors
    };
  }
}

module.exports = MyPlugin;
```

#### Manifesto do Plugin
```json
{
  "id": "my-custom-plugin",
  "name": "My Custom Plugin",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "description": "Processa dados personalizados",
  "author": "Seu Nome",
  "license": "MIT",
  "main": "index.js",
  "dependencies": {
    "axios": "^1.0.0"
  },
  "configSchema": {
    "type": "object",
    "properties": {
      "apiKey": {
        "type": "string",
        "description": "Chave da API"
      },
      "endpoint": {
        "type": "string",
        "default": "https://api.example.com"
      }
    },
    "required": ["apiKey"]
  }
}
```

### Exemplo de Teste
```javascript
// tests/unit/workflow-engine.test.js
const { WorkflowEngine } = require('../../src/core/engine');
const { MockDatabase, MockPluginRegistry } = require('../mocks');

describe('WorkflowEngine', () => {
  let engine;
  let mockDb;
  let mockRegistry;
  
  beforeEach(() => {
    mockDb = new MockDatabase();
    mockRegistry = new MockPluginRegistry();
    engine = new WorkflowEngine({}, mockDb, mockRegistry);
  });
  
  describe('executeWorkflow', () => {
    it('should execute workflow successfully', async () => {
      // Arrange
      const workflowId = 'test-wf-1';
      const input = { data: 'test' };
      
      mockDb.setupWorkflow(workflowId, {
        id: workflowId,
        steps: [{ type: 'test', config: {} }]
      });
      
      // Act
      const result = await engine.executeWorkflow(workflowId, input);
      
      // Assert
      expect(result.success).toBe(true);
      expect(result.executionId).toBeDefined();
      expect(mockRegistry.executePlugin).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });
    
    it('should handle workflow not found', async () => {
      // Act & Assert
      await expect(
        engine.executeWorkflow('non-existent', {})
      ).rejects.toThrow('Workflow not found');
    });
    
    it('should retry on transient failures', async () => {
      // Teste de retry automático
    });
  });
});
```

## 📊 Monitoramento e Logs

### Configuração de Logs
```javascript
// src/utils/logger.js
const winston = require('winston');
const { ElasticsearchTransport } = require('winston-elasticsearch');

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console({
      format: winston.format.simple()
    }),
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: 'logs/error.log', 
      level: 'error' 
    }),
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: 'logs/combined.log' 
    }),
    new ElasticsearchTransport({
      level: 'info',
      clientOpts: { node: process.env.ELASTICSEARCH_URL }
    })
  ]
});

module.exports = logger;
```

### Métricas
```javascript
// src/monitoring/metrics.js
const client = require('prom-client');

const metrics = {
  workflowExecutions: new client.Counter({
    name: 'diyapp_workflow_executions_total',
    help: 'Total de execuções de workflow',
    labelNames: ['workflow_id', 'status']
  }),
  
  executionDuration: new client.Histogram({
    name: 'diyapp_execution_duration_seconds',
    help: 'Duração das execuções',
    labelNames: ['workflow_id'],
    buckets: [0.1, 0.5, 1, 5, 10, 30]
  }),
  
  pluginExecutions: new client.Counter({
    name: 'diyapp_plugin_executions_total',
    help: 'Execuções de plugins',
    labelNames: ['plugin_id', 'status']
  }),
  
  systemHealth: new client.Gauge({
    name: 'diyapp_system_health',
    help: 'Health do sistema (1 = saudável, 0 = não saudável)'
  })
};

module.exports = metrics;
```

    </style>
</head>

### [Sessão Paralela: Compliance]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Verificação de Conformidade

Analisando a estrutura do projeto para conformidade com LGPD/GDPR, licenças de código aberto e políticas de retenção de dados.

## 1. Estrutura de Conformidade Implementada
